  <text xml:lang="sa-Latn">

    <body>
      <div n="6" type="sthāna">

        <head>[uttaratantram]</head>

        

        <div n="39" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ekonacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.1"> athāto jvarapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.3.1"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.3"> yenāmṛtam apāṃ madhyād uddhṛtaṃ pūrvajanmani |
            <caesura/>
             yato 'maratvaṃ saṃprāptās tridaśās tridiveśvarāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.4"> śiṣyās taṃ devam āsīnaṃ papracchuḥ suśrutādayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇasyopadravāḥ proktā vraṇinām apy ataḥ param || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.5"> samāsād vyāsataś caiva brūhi no bhiṣajāṃ vara |
            <caesura/>
             upadraveṇa juṣṭasya vraṇaḥ kṛcchreṇa sidhyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.6"> upadravās tu vraṇinaḥ kṛcchrasādhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya śeṣadhātuparikṣayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.7ab"> tasmād upadravān kṛtsnān brūhi naḥ sacikitsitān | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.7cd"> sarvakāyacikitsāsu ye dṛṣṭāḥ paramarṣiṇā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.8"> teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā prābravīd bhiṣajāṃ varaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jvaram ādau pravakṣyāmi sa rogānīkarāṭ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.9"> rudrakopāgnisaṃbhūtaḥ sarvabhūtapratāpanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tais tair nāmabhir anyeṣāṃ sattvānāṃ parikīrtyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.10"> janmādau nidhane caiva prāyo viśati dehinam |
            <caesura/>
             ataḥ sarvavikārāṇām ayaṃ rājā prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.11"> ṛte devamanuṣyebhyo nānyo viṣahate tu tam |
            <caesura/>
             karmaṇā labhate yasmād devatvaṃ mānusād api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.12"> punaś caiva cyutaḥ svargān mānuṣyam anuvartate |
            <caesura/>
             tasmāt te devabhāvena sahante mānuṣā jvaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.13"> śeṣāḥ sarve vipadyante tairyagyonā jvarārditāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             svedāvarodhaḥ santāpaḥ sarvāṅgagrahaṇaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.14"> vikārā yugapad yasmin jvaraḥ sa parikīrtitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             doṣaiḥ pṛthak samastaiś ca dvandvair āgantur eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.15"> anekakāraṇotpannaḥ smṛtas tv aṣṭavidho jvaraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             doṣāḥ prakupitāḥ sveṣu kāleṣu svaiḥ prakopaṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.16"> vyāpya deham aśeṣeṇa jvaram āpādayanti hi |
            <caesura/>
             duṣṭāḥ svahetubhir doṣāḥ prāpyām āśayam ūṣmaṇā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.17"> sahitā rasam āgatya rasasvedapravāhiṇām |
            <caesura/>
             srotasāṃ mārgam āvṛtya mandīkṛtya hutāśanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.18"> nirasya bahir ūṣmāṇaṃ paktisthānāc ca kevalam |
            <caesura/>
             śarīraṃ samabhivyāpya svakāleṣu jvarāgamam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.19ab"> janayaty atha vṛddhiṃ vā svavarṇaṃ ca tvagādiṣu |</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.19cd"> mithyāti<pc> </pc>yuktair api ca snehādyaiḥ karmabhir
            nṛṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.20"> vividhād abhighātāc ca rogotthānāt prapākataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śramāt kṣayād ajīrṇāc ca viṣāt sātmyartuparyayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.21"> oṣadhīpuṣpagandhāc ca śokān nakṣatrapīḍayā |
            <caesura/>
             abhicārābhiśāpābhyāṃ manobhūtābhiśaṅkayā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.22"> strīṇām apaprajātānāṃ prajātānāṃ tathāhitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             stanyāvataraṇe caiva jvaro doṣaiḥ pravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.23"> tair vegavadbhir bahudhā samudbhrāntair vimārgagaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vikṣipyamāṇo 'ntaragnir bhavaty āśu bahiś caraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.24"> ruṇaddhi cāpy apāṃ dhātuṃ yasmāt tasmāj jvarāturaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhavaty atyuṣṇagātraś ca jvaritastena cocyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.25"> śramo 'ratirvivarṇatvaṃ vairasyaṃ nayanaplavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             icchādveṣau muhuś cāpi śītavātātapādiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.26"> jṛmbhāṅgamardo gurutā romaharṣo 'rucis tamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             apraharṣaś ca śītaṃ ca bhavaty utpatsyati jvare || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.27"> sāmānyato viśeṣāt tu jṛmbhātyarthaṃ samīraṇāt |
            <caesura/>
             pittānnayanayor dāhaḥ kaphānnannābhinandanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.28"> sarvaliṅgasamavāyaḥ sarvadoṣaprakopaje |
            <caesura/>
             dvayor dvayos tu rūpeṇa saṃsṛṣṭaṃ dvandvajaṃ viduḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.29"> vepathur viṣamo vegaḥ kaṇṭhauṣṭhapariśoṣaṇam |
            <caesura/>
             nidrānāśaḥ kṣutaḥ stambho gātrāṇāṃ raukṣyam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.30"> śirohṛdgātrarugvaktravairasyaṃ baddhaviṭkatā |
            <caesura/>
             jṛmbhādhmānṃa tathā śūlaṃ bhavaty anilaje jvare || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.31"> vegastīkṣṇo 'tisāraś ca nidrālpatvaṃ tathā vamiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇṭhauṣṭhamukhanāsānāṃ pākaḥ svedaś ca jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.32"> pralāpaḥ kaṭutā vaktre mūrcchā dāho madastṛṣā |
            <caesura/>
             pītaviṇmūtranetratvaṃ paittike bhrama eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.33"> gauravaṃ śītamutkleśo romaharṣo 'tinidratā |
            <caesura/>
             srotorodho rugalpatvaṃ praseko madhurāsyatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.34"> nātyuṣṇagātratā chardiraṅgasādo 'vipākatā |
            <caesura/>
             pratiśyāyo 'ruciḥ kāsaḥ kaphaje 'kṣṇoś ca śuklatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.35"> nidrānāśo bhramaḥ śvāsastandrā suptāṅgatāruciḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tṛṣṇā moho madaḥ stambho dāhaḥ śītaṃ hṛdi vyathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.36"> paktiś cireṇa doṣāṇāmunmādaḥ śyāvadantatā |
            <caesura/>
             rasanā paruṣā kṛṣṇā sandhimūrdhāsthijā rujaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.37"> nirbhugne kaluṣe netre karṇau śabdaruganvitau |
            <caesura/>
             pralāpaḥ srotasāṃ pākaḥ kūjanaṃ cetanācyutiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.38"> svedamūtrapurīṣāṇām alpaśaḥ sucirāt srutiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarvaje sarvaliṅgāni viśeṣaṃ cātra me śṛṇu ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.39"> nātyuṣṇaśīto 'lpasaṃjño bhrāntaprekṣī hatasvaraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kharajihvaḥ śuṣkakaṇṭhaḥ svedaviṇmūtravarjitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.40"> sāsro nirbhugnahṛdayo bhaktadveṣī hataprabhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śvasannipatitaḥ śete pralāpopadravāyutaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.41"> tam abhinyāsam ity āhur hataujasam athāpare |
            <caesura/>
             sannipātajvaraṃ kṛcchram asādhyam apare viduḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.42"> nidropetam abhinyāsaṃ kṣīṇamenaṃ hataujasam |
            <caesura/>
             saṃnyastagātraṃ saṃnyāsaṃ vidyāt sarvātmake jvare || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.43"> ojo visraṃsate yasya pittānilasamucchrayāt |
            <caesura/>
             sa gātrastambhaśītābhyāṃ śayanepsuracetanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.44"> api jāgrat svapan jantustandrāluś ca pralāpavān |
            <caesura/>
             saṃhṛṣṭaromā srastāṅgo mandasantāpavedanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.45"> ojonirodhajaṃ tasya jānīyāt kuśalo bhis ak |
            <caesura/>
             saptame vidase prāpte daśame dvādaśe 'pi vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.46"> punar dhorataro bhūtvā praśamaṃ yāti hanti vā |
            <caesura/>
             dvidoṣocchrāyaliṅgās tu dvandvajās trividhāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.47"> tṛṣṇā mūrcchā bhramo dāhaḥ svapnanāśaḥ śirorujā |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇṭhāsyaśoṣo vamathū romaharṣo 'rucis tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.48"> parvbhedaś ca jṛmbhā ca vātapittajvarākṛtiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             staimityaṃ parvaṇaṃ bhedo nidrā gauravam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.49"> śirograhaḥ pratiśyāyaḥ kāsaḥ svedapravartanam |
            <caesura/>
             santāpo madhyavegaś ca vātaśleṣmajvarākṛtiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.50ab"> liptātiktāsyatā tandrā mohaḥ kāso 'rucistṛṣā |
            <caesura/>
             muhurdāho muhuḥ śītaṃ śleṣmapittajvarākṛtiḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.50.1"> ( |
            <caesura/>
             jṛmbhādhmānamadotkampaparvabhedaparikṣayāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tṛṭpralāpābhitāpāḥ syurjvare mārutapaittike || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.50.2"> śūlakāsakakotkleśaśītavepathupīnasāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gauravāruciviṣṭambhā vātaśleṣmasamudbhave || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.50.3"> śītadāhārucistambhasvedamohamadabhramāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kāsāṅgasādahṛllāsā bhavanti kaphapaittike ||) </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.51"> kṛśānāṃ jvaramuktānāṃ mithyāhāravihāriṇām |
            <caesura/>
             doṣaḥ svalpo 'pi saṃvṛddho dehinām anileritaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.52"> satatānyed yuṣkatryākhyacāturthān sapralepakān |
            <caesura/>
             kaphasthānavibhāgena yathāsaṃkhyaṃ karoti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.53"> ahorātrādahorātrāt sthānāt sthānaṃ prapadyate |
            <caesura/>
             tataś cāmāśayaṃ prāpya doṣaḥ kuryājjvaraṃ nṛṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.54"> tathā pralepako jñeyaḥ śoṣiṇāṃ prāṇanāśanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             duścikitsyatamo mandaḥ sukaṣṭo dhātuśoṣakṛt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.55"> kaphasthāneṣu vā doṣastiṣṭan dvitricaturṣu vā |
            <caesura/>
             viparyayākhyān kurute viṣamān kṛcchrasādhanān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.56"> paro hetuḥ svabhāvo vā viṣame kaiś cidīritaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             āgantuś canubandho hi prāyaśo viṣamajvare || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.57"> vātādhikatvāt pravadanti tajjñāstṛtīyakaṃ cāpi
            caturthakaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             aupatyake madyasamudbhave ca hetuṃ jvare pittakṛtaṃ vadanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.58"> pralepakaṃ vātabalāsakaṃ ca kaphādhikatvena vadanti
            tajjñāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūrcchānubandhā viṣam ajvarā ye prāyeṇa te dvandvasamutthitās tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.59"> tvaksthau śleṣmānilau śītamādau janayato jvare |
            <caesura/>
             tayoḥ praśāntayoḥ pittamante dāhaṃ karoti ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.60"> karoty ādau tathā pittaṃ tvaksthaṃ dāham atīva ca |
            <caesura/>
             praśānte kurutas tasmiṃś chītam ante ca tāv api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.61"> dvāv etau dāhaśītādī jvarau saṃsargajau smṛtau |
            <caesura/>
             dāhapūrvas tayoḥ kaṣṭaḥ kṛcchrasādhyaś ca sa smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.62ab"> prasaktaś cābhighātotthaś cetanāprabhavas tu yaḥ | </l>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.62cd"> rātryahnoḥ ṣaṭsu kāleṣu kīrtiteṣu tathā purā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.63"> prasahya viṣamo 'bhyeti mānavaṃ bahudhā jvaraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sa cāpi viṣamo dehaṃ na kadācidvimuñcati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.64"> glānigauravakārśyebhyaḥ sa yasmān na pramucyate |
            <caesura/>
             vege tu samatikrānte gato 'yam iti lakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.65"> dhātvantarastho līnatvān na saukṣmyādupalabhyate |
            <caesura/>
             alpadoṣendhanaḥ kṣīṇaḥ kṣīṇendhana ivānalaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.66"> doṣo 'lpo 'hitasaṃbhūto jvarotsṛṣṭasya vā punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dhātum anyatamaṃ prāpya karoti viṣamajvaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.67"> satataṃ rasaraktasthaḥ so 'nyed yuḥ piśitāśritaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             medogatas tṛtīye 'hni tv asthimajjagataḥ punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.68ab"> kuryāc cāturthakaṃ ghoram antakaṃ rogasaṃkaram |</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.68cd"> kecidbhūtābhiṣaṅgotthaṃ bruvate viṣamajvaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.69"> saptāhaṃ vā daśāhaṃ vā dvādaśāham athāpi vā |
            <caesura/>
             santatyā yo 'visargī syāt santataḥ sa nigadyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.70"> ahorātre satatako dvau kālāvanuvartate |
            <caesura/>
             anyed yuṣkastvahorātrādekakālaṃ pravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.71"> tṛtīyakastṛtīye 'hni caturthe 'hni caturthakaḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.255"> pañcasāram idaṃpeyaṃ mathitaṃ viṣamajvare |
            <caesura/>
             kṣatakṣīṇe kṣaye śvāse hṛdroge caitadiṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.256"> lākṣāviśvaniśāmūrvāmañjiṣṭhāsvarjikāmayaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ṣaḍguṇena ca takreṇa siddhaṃ tailaṃ jvarāntakṛt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.257"> kṣīrivṛkṣāsanāriṣṭajambūsaptacchadārjunaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śirīṣakhadirāsphoṭāmṛtavallyāṭarūṣakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.258"> kaṭukāparpaṭośīravacātejovatīghanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sādhitaṃ tailamabhyaṅgādāśu jīrṇajvarāpaham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.259"> nirviṣairbhujagairnāgairvinītaiḥ kṛtataskaraiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             trāsayed āgame cainaṃ tad ahar bhojayen na ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.260"> atyabhiṣyandigurubhir vāmayed vā punaḥ punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             madyaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ pāyayeta ghṛtaṃ vā jvaranāśanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.261"> purāṇaṃ vā ghṛtaṃ kāmamudāraṃ vā virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             nirūhayed vā matimān susvinnaṃ tad ahari naram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.262"> ajāvyoś carmaromāṇi vacā kuṣṭhaṃ palaṅkaṣā |
            <caesura/>
             nimbapatraṃ madhuyutaṃ dhūpanaṃ tasya dāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.263"> baiḍālaṃ vā śakṛdyojyaṃ vepamānasya dhūpanam |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.264"> udaroktāni sarpīṣi yānyuktāni purā mayā |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.265"> bhūtavidyāsamuddiṣṭairbandhāveśanapūjanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.266"> śramakṣayotthe bhuñjīta ghṛtābhyakto rasaudanam |
            <caesura/>
             abhiśāpābhicārotthau jvarau homādinā jayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.267"> dānasvastyayanātithyair utpātagrahapīḍitam |
            <caesura/>
             abhighātajvare kuryāt kriyāmuṣṇavivarjitām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.268"> kaṣāyamadhurāṃ snigdhāṃ yathādoṣam athāpi vā |
            <caesura/>
             auṣadhīgandhaviṣajau viṣapittaprasādhanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.269"> jayet kaṣāyaṃ ca hitaṃ sarvagandhakṛtaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             nimbadārukaṣāyaṃ vā hitaṃ saumanasaṃ yathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.270"> yavānnavikṛtiḥ sarpirmadyaṃ ca viṣame hitam |
            <caesura/>
             saṃpūjayed vijān gāś ca devamīśānamambikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.271"> kaphavātotthayoś cāpi jvarayoḥ śītapīḍitam |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.272"> siñcet koṣṇairāranālaśuktagomūtramastubhiḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.274"> avagāhaḥ sukhoṣṇaś ca vātaghnakvāthayojitaḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.275"> praveśyaurṇikakārpāsakauśeyāmbarasaṃvṛtam |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.278"> pralambabimbapracaladbimbīphalanibhādharāḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.280"> gāḍhamāliṅgayeyustaṃ taruṃ vanalatā iva |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.281"> tāsāmaṅgapariṣvaṅganivārutahimajvaram |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.282"> dāhābhibhūte tu vidhiṃ kuryād dāhavināśanam |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.283"> dāhajvarārtaṃ matimān vāmayet kṣipram eva ca |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.284"> kolāmalakasaṃyuktaiḥ śuktadhānyāmlasaṃyutaiḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.286"> lipte 'ṅge dāhatṛṇmūrcchāḥ praśāmyanti ca sarvaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.287"> amlaprasthaśatonmiśraṃ tailaprasthaṃ vipācayet |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.288"> nyagrodhādirgaṇo yas tu kākolyādiś ca yo gaṇaḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.289"> tatkaṣāyāmlasaṃsiddhāḥ snehāś cābhyañjane hitāḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.290"> dāhavege tv atikrānte tasmād uddhṛtya mānavam |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.292"> bibhratyo 'bjasrajaś citrā maṇiratnavibhūṣitāḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.293"> prahlādaṃ cāsya vijñāya tāḥ strīr apanayet punaḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.294"> pittajvaroktaṃ śamanaṃ vireko 'nyad dhitaṃ ca yat |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.300"> madhūkam atha hrīberam utpalāni madhūlikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.301"> līḍvā cūrṇāni madhunā sarpiṣā ca jayed vamim |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.303"> vidārī dāḍimaṃ lodhraṃ dadhitthaṃ bījapūrakam |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.304"> dāḍimasya sitāyāś ca drākṣāmalakayos tathā |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.305"> kṣīrekṣurasamākṣīkasarpistailoṣṇavāribhiḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.307"> pakve pittajvare rakte cordhvage vepathau tathā |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.308"> hṛtadoṣo bhramārtas tu lihyāt kṣaudrasitābhayāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vātaghnamadhurairyojyā nirūhā vātaje jvare || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.309"> avekṣya doṣaṃ prāṇaṃ ca yathāsvaṃ cānuvāsanāḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.311"> gairikāñjanamañjiṣṭhāmṛṇālānyatha padmakam |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.312"> supūtaṃ śītalaṃ bastiṃ dahyamānāya dāpayet |
            <caesura/>
             jvaradāhāpahaṃ teṣu siddhaṃ caivānuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.313"> āragvadhagaṇakvāthāḥ pippalyādisamāyutāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sakṣaudramūtrā deyāḥ syuḥ kaphajvaravināśanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.314"> kaphaghnair eva saṃsiddhā dravyaiś cāpy anuvāsanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saṃsarge sannipāte ca saṃsṛṣṭā bastayo hitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.315"> saṃsṛṣṭair eva saṃsṛṣṭā dravyaiś cāpy anuvāsanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vātarogāpahāḥ sarve snehā ye samyag īritāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.316"> vinā tailaṃ ta eva syuryojyā mārutaje jvare |
            <caesura/>
             nikhilenopayojyāś ca ta evābhyañjanādiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.317"> paittike madhurais tiktaiḥ siddhaṃ sarpiś ca pūjyate |
            <caesura/>
             ślaiṣmike kaṭutiktaiś ca saṃsṛṣṭānītareṣu ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.318"> hṛtāvaśeṣaṃ pittaṃ tu tvaksthaṃ janayati jvaram |
            <caesura/>
             pibed ikṣurasaṃ tatra śītaṃ vā śarkarodakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.319"> śāliṣaṣṭikayor annam aśnīyāt kṣīrasaṃplutam |
            <caesura/>
             kaphavātotthayor eva svedābhyaṅgau prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.320"> ghṛtaṃ dvādaśarātrāt tu deyaṃ sarvajvareṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             tenāntareṇāśayaṃ svaṃ gatā doṣā bhavanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.321"> dhānūn prakṣobhayan doṣo mokṣakāle balīyate |
            <caesura/>
             tena vyākulacittas tu mriyamāṇa ivehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.322"> laghutvaṃ śirasaḥ svedo mukhamāpāṇḍu pāki ca |
            <caesura/>
             kṣavathuś cānnakāṅkṣā ca jvaram uktasya lakṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.323"> śambhukrodhodbhavo ghoro balavarṇāgnisādakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rogarāṭ roghasaṃghāto jvara ity upadiśyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.324"> vyāpitvāt sarvasaṃsparśāt kṛcchratvād antasaṃbhavāt |
            <caesura/>
             antako hy eṣa bhūtānāṃ jvara ity upadiśyate ||</l>

          <head>catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.1"> athāto 'tīsārapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.3"> gurvatisnigdharūkṣoṣṇadravasthūlātiśītalaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viruddhādhyaśanājīrṇairasātmyaiś cāpi bhojanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.4"> snehādyairatiyuktaiś ca mithyāyuktairviṣādbhayāt |
            <caesura/>
             śokādduṣṭāmbumadyātipānāt sātmyartuparyayāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.5"> jalātiramaṇairvegavighātaiḥ kṛmidoṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nṛṇāṃ bhavaty atīsāro lakṣaṇaṃ tasya vakṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.6"> saṃśamyāpāṃdhāturantaḥ kṛśānuṃ varcomiśro mārutena
            praṇunnaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vṛddho 'tīvādhaḥ saratyeṣa yasmādvyādhiṃ ghoraṃ taṃ tvatīsāram āhuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.7"> ekaikaśaḥ sarvaśaś cāpi doṣaiḥ śokenānyaḥ ṣaṣṭha āmena
            coktaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kecit prāhurnaikarūpaprakāraṃ naivety evaṃ kāśirājastvavocat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.8"> doṣāvasthāstasya naikaprakārāḥ kāle kāle
            vyādhitasyodbhavanti |
            <caesura/>
             hṛnnābhipāyūdarakukṣitodagātrāvasādānilasannirodhāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.9"> viṭsaṅga ādhmānamathāvipāko bhaviṣyatas tasya puraḥsarāṇi
            |
            <caesura/>
             śūlāviṣṭaḥ saktamūtro 'ntrakūjī srastāpānaḥ sannakaṭyūrugaṅghaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.10"> varco muñcatyalpamalpaṃ saphenaṃ rūkṣaṃ śyāvaṃ sānilaṃ
            mārutena |
            <caesura/>
             durgandhyuṣṇaṃ vegavanmāṃsatoyaprakhyaṃ bhinnaṃ svinnadeho 'titīkṣṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.11"> pittāt pītaṃ nīlamālohitaṃ vā
            tṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhapākajvarārtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tandrānidrāgauravotkleśasadīvegāśaṅkī sṛṣṭaviṭko 'pi bhūyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.12"> śuklaṃ sāndraṃ śleṣmaṇā śleṣmayuktaṃ bhaktadveṣī
            niḥsvanaṃ hṛṣṭaromā |
            <caesura/>
             tandrāyukto mohasādāsyaśoṣī varcaḥ kuryānnaikavarṇaṃ tṛṣārtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.13"> sarvodbhūte sarvaliṅgopapattiḥ kṛcchraś cāyaṃ
            bālavṛddheṣv asādhyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tais tairbhāvaiḥ paktimāvidhya(āviśya)jantoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.14"> koṣṭhaṃ gatvā kṣobhayatyasya raktaṃ taccādhastāt
            kākaṇantīprakāśam |
            <caesura/>
             varcomiśraṃ niḥpurīṣaṃ sagandhaṃ nirgandhaṃ vā sāryate tena kṛcchrāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.15"> śokotpanno duścikitsyo 'timātraṃ rogo vaidyaiḥ kaṣṭa eṣa
            pradiṣṭaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             āmājīrṇopadrutāḥ kṣobhayantaḥ koṣṭhaṃ doṣāḥ saṃpraduṣṭāḥ sabhaktam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.16"> nānāvarṇaṃ naikaśaḥ sārayanti kṛcchrājjantoḥ ṣaṣṭhamenaṃ
            vadanti | </l>
          <l/>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.17"> saṃsṛṣṭamebhir doṣaistu nyastamapsvavasīdati |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.20"> rājīmadvā candrakaiḥ santataṃ vā pūyaprakhyaṃ

            <caesura/>
             hanyādetadyat pratīpaṃ bhavec ca kṣīṇaṃ hanyuś copasargāḥ prabhūtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.21"> asaṃvṛtagudaṃ kṣīṇaṃ durādhmātam upadrutam |
            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.23"> snehājīrṇanimittas tu bahuśūlapravāhikaḥ |

            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.44"> hiṅgurvatsakabījāni vacā bilvaśalāṭu ca |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.102"> hitaḥ snehavireko vā bastayaḥ picchilāś ca ye |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.103"> śakṛtā yas tu saṃsṛṣṭamatisāryeta śoṇitam |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.104"> kṣīriśuṅgāśṛtaṃ sarpiḥ pibet sakṣaudraśarkaram |

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.105"> saṃyuktaṃ bhadrarohiṇyā pakvaṃ peyādimiśritam |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.106"> gaurave vamanaṃ pathyaṃ yasya syāt prabalaḥ kaphaḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.107"> saṃpakve bahudoṣe ca vibandhe mūtraśodhanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.108"> pravāhaṇe gudabhraṃśe mūtrāghāte kaṭigrahe |
            <caesura/>
             madhurāmlaiḥ śṛtaṃ tailaṃ sarpir vāpy anuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.109"> gudapākas tu pittena yasya syādahitāśinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasya pittaharāḥ sekāstatsiddhāś cānuvāsanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.110"> dadhimaṇḍasurābilvasiddhaṃ tailaṃ samārute |
            <caesura/>
             bhojane ca hitaṃ kṣīraṃ kacchurāmūlasādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.111"> alpālpaṃ bahuśo raktaṃ sarugya upaveśyate |
            <caesura/>
             yadā vāyur vibaddhaś ca picchābastis tadā hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.112"> prāyeṇa gudadaurbalyaṃ dīrghakālātisāriṇām |
            <caesura/>
             bhavettasmād dhitaṃ teṣāṃ gude tailāvacāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.113"> kapitthaśālmalīphañjīvaṭakārpāsadāḍimāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yūthikā kacchurā śeluḥ śaṇaś cuccūś ca dādhikāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.114"> śālaparṇī pṛśniparṇī bṛhatī kaṇṭakārikā |
            <caesura/>
             balāśvadaṃṣṭrābilvāni pāṭhānāgaradhānyakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.115"> eṣa āhārasaṃyoge hitaḥ sarvātisāriṇām |
            <caesura/>
             tilakalko hitaś cātra maudgo mudgarasas tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.116"> pittātisārī yo martyaḥ pittalāny atiṣevate |
            <caesura/>
             pittaṃ praduṣṭaṃ tasyāśu raktātīsārabhāvahet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.117"> jvaraṃ śūlaṃ tṛṣāṃ dāhaṃ gudapākaṃ ca dāruṇam |
            <caesura/>
             yo raktaṃ śakṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ paścād vā pratisāryate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.118"> sa pallavairvaṭādīnaṃ sasarpiḥ sādhitaṃ payaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pibet saśarkarākṣaudramathavāpyabhimathya tat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.119"> navanītamatho lihyāttakraṃ cānupibettataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             priyālaśālmalīplakṣaśallakītiniśatvacaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.120"> kṣīre vimṛditāḥ pītāḥ sakṣaudrā raktanāśanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             madhukaṃ śarkarāṃ lodhraṃ payasyāmatha sārivām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.121"> pibec chāgena payasā sakṣaudraṃ raktanāśanam |
            <caesura/>
             mañjiṣṭhāṃ sārivāṃ lodhraṃ padmakaṃ kumudotpalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.122"> pibet padmāṃ ca dugdhena chāgenāsṛkpraśāntaye |
            <caesura/>
             śarkarotpalalodhrāṇi samaṅgā madhukaṃ tilāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.123"> tilāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ sayaṣṭyāhvāḥ samaṅgā cotpalāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             tilā mocaraso lodhraṃ tathaiva madhukotpalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.124"> kacchurā tilakalkaś ca yogāś catvāra eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             ājena payasā peyāḥ sarakte madhusaṃyutāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.125"> drave sarakte sravati bālabilvaṃ saphāṇitam |
            <caesura/>
             sakṣaudratailaṃ prāgeva lihyādāśu hitaṃ hi tat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.126"> kośakāraṃ ghṛte bhṛṣṭaṃ lājacūrṇaṃ sitā madhu |
            <caesura/>
             saśūlaṃ raktapittotthaṃ līḍhaṃ hantyudarāmayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.127"> bilvamadhyaṃ samadhukaṃ śarkarākṣaudrasaṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             taṇḍulāmbuyuto yogaḥ pittaraktotthitaṃ jayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.128"> yogān sāṃgrāhikāṃś cānyān pibetsakṣaudraśarkarān |
            <caesura/>
             nyagrodhādiṣu kuryāc ca puṭapākān yatheritān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.129"> gudāpāke ca ye uktāste 'trāpi vidhayaḥ smṛtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rujāyāṃ cāpraśāmyantyāṃ picchāvastirhito bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.130"> saktaviḍ doṣabahulaṃ dīptāgniryo 'tisāryate |
            <caesura/>
             viḍaṅgatriphalākṛṣṇākaṣāyais taṃ virecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.131"> athavairaṇḍasiddhena payasā kevalena vā |
            <caesura/>
             yavāgūrvitareccāsya vātaghnairdīpanaiḥ kṛtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.132"> dīptāgnirniṣpurīṣo yaḥ sāryate phenilaṃ śakṛt |
            <caesura/>
             sa pibet phāṇitaṃ śuṇṭhīdadhitailapayoghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.133"> svinnāni guḍatailābhyāṃ bhakṣayed badarāṇi ca |
            <caesura/>
             svinnāni piṣṭavadvāpi samaṃ bilvaśalāṭubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.134"> dadhnopayujya kulmāṣān śvetāmanupibet surām |
            <caesura/>
             śaśamāṃsaṃ sarudhiraṃ samaṅgāṃ saghṛtaṃ dadhi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.135"> khādedvipācya seveta mṛdvannaṃ śakṛtaḥ kṣaye |
            <caesura/>
             saṃskṛto yamake māṣayavakolarasaḥ śubhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.136"> bhojanārthaṃ pradātavyo dadhidāḍimasādhitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viḍaṃ bilvaśalāṭūni nāgaraṃ cāmlapeṣitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.137"> dadhnaḥ saraś ca yamake bhṛṣṭo varcaḥkṣaye hitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saśūlaṃ kṣīṇavarcā yo dīptāgniratisāryate |
            <caesura/>
             sa pibeddīpanairyuktaṃ sarpiḥ saṃgrāhakaiḥ saha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.138"> vāyuḥ pravṛddho nicitaṃ balāsaṃ
            nudatyadhastādahitāśanasya |
            <caesura/>
             pravāhamāṇasya muhurmalāktaṃ pravāhikāṃ tāṃ pravadanti tajjñāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.139"> pravāhikā vātakṛtā saśūlā pittāt sadāhā sakaphā kaphāc
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             saśoṇitā śoṇitasaṃbhavā tu tāḥ sneharūkṣaprabhavā matās tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.140"> tāsāmatīsāravadādiśec ca liṅgaṃ kramaṃ cāmavipakvatāṃ
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             na śāntimāyāti vilaṅghanairyā yogair udīrṇā yadi pācanair vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.141"> tāṃ kṣīramevāśu śṛtaṃ nihanti tailaṃ tilāḥ
            picchilabastayaś ca |
            <caesura/>
             ārdraiḥ kuśaiḥ saṃpariveṣṭitāni vṛntānyathārdrāṇi hi śālmalīnām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.142"> pkvāni samyak puṭapākayogenāpothya tebhyo rasamādadīta
            |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ tailahavirvimiśraṃ kalkena yaṣṭīmadhukasya vāpi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.143"> bastiṃ vidadhyādbhiṣagapramattaḥ
            pravāhikāmūtrapurīṣasaṅge |
            <caesura/>
             dvipañjcamūlīkvathitena śūle pravāhamāṇasya samākṣikeṇa || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.144"> kṣīreṇa cāsthāpanamagryamuktaṃ tailena
            yuñjyādanuvāsanaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             vātaghnavarge lavaṇeṣu caiva tailaṃ ca siddhaṃ hitamannapāne || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.145"> lodhraṃ viḍaṃ bilvaśalāṭu caiva lihyāc ca tailena
            kaṭutrikāḍhyam |
            <caesura/>
             dadhnā sasāreṇa samākṣikeṇa bhuñjīta niś cāraka(niḥsāraka))pīḍitas tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.146"> sutaptakupyakvathitena vāpi kṣīreṇa śītena madhuplutena
            |
            <caesura/>
             śūlārdito vyoṣavidārigandhāsiddhena dugdhena hitāya bhojyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.147"> vātaghnasaṃgrāhikadīpanīyaiḥ kṛtān ṣaḍāṃś cāpy
            upabhojayec ca |
            <caesura/>
             khādec ca matsyān rasamāpnuyāc ca vātaghnasiddhaṃ saghṛtaṃ satailam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.148"> eṇāvyajānāṃ tu vaṭapravālaiḥ siddhāni sārdhaṃ piśitāni
            khādet |
            <caesura/>
             medhyasya(medyasya) siddhaṃ tvatha vāpi raktaṃ bastasya dadhnā
            ghṛtatailayuktam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.149"> khādet pradehaiḥ śikhilāvajair vā bhuñjīta
            yūṣairdadhibhiś ca mukhyaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             māṣān susiddhān ghṛtamaṇḍayuktān khādec ca dadhnā maricopadaṃśān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.150"> mahāruje mūtrakṛcchre bhiṣag bastiṃ pradāpayet |
            <caesura/>
             payomadhughṛtonmiśraṃ madhukotpalasādhitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.151"> sa bastiḥ śamayettasya raktaṃ dāhamatho jvaram |
            <caesura/>
             madhurauṣadhasiddhaṃ ca hitaṃ tasyānuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.152"> rātrāvahani vā nityaṃ rujārto yo bhaven naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā yathā satailaḥ syādvātaśāntis tathā tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.153"> praśānte mārute cāpi śāntiṃ yāti pravāhikā |
            <caesura/>
             tasmāt pravāhikāroge mārutaṃ śamayed bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.154"> pāṭhājamodākuṭajotpalaṃ ca śuṇṭhī samā māgadhikāś ca
            piṣṭāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sukhāmbupītāḥ śamayanti rogaṃ medhyāṇḍasiddhaṃ saghṛtaṃ payo vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.155"> śuṇṭhīṃ ghṛtaṃ sakṣavakaṃ satailaṃ vipācya līḍhvāmayam
            āśu hanyāt |
            <caesura/>
             gajāśanākumbhikadāḍimānāṃ rasaiḥ kṛtā tailaghṛte sadadhni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.156"> bilvānvitā pathyatamā yavāgūrdhāroṣṇadugdhasya tathā ca
            pānam |
            <caesura/>
             laghūni pathyānyatha dīpanāni snigdhāni bhojyānyudarāmayeṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.157"> hitāya nityaṃ vitaredvibhajya yogāṃś ca tāṃstān
            bhiṣagapramattaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.158"> tṛṣṇāpanayanī laghvī dīpanī bastiśodhanī |
            <caesura/>
             jvare caivātisāre ca yavāgūḥ sarvadā hitā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.159"> rūkṣājjāte kriyā snigdhā rūkṣā snehanimittaje |
            <caesura/>
             bhayaje sāntvanāpūrvā śokaje śokanāśinī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.160"> viṣārśaḥkṛmisaṃbhūte hitā cobhayaśarmadā |
            <caesura/>
             chardimūrcchātṛḍādyāṃś ca sādhayed avirodhataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.161"> samavāye tu doṣāṇāṃ pūrvaṃ pittamupācaret |
            <caesura/>
             jvare caivātisāre ca sarvatrānyatra mārutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.162"> yasyoccāraṃ vinā mūtraṃ samyag vāyuś ca gacchati |
            <caesura/>
             dīptāgnerlaghukoṣṭhasya sthitastasyodarāmayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.163"> karmajā vyādhayaḥ keciddoṣajāḥ santi cāpare |
            <caesura/>
             karmadoṣodbhavāś cānye karmajāsteṣv ahetukāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.164"> naśyanti tvakriyābhis te kriyābhiḥ karmasaṃkṣaye |
            <caesura/>
             śāmyanti doṣasaṃbhūtā doṣasaṃkṣayahetubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.165"> teṣāmalpanidānā ye pratikaṣṭā bhavanti ca |
            <caesura/>
             mṛdavo bahudoṣā vā karmadoṣodbhavās tu te || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.166"> karmadoṣakṣayakṛtā teṣāṃ siddhirvidhīyate |
            <caesura/>
             duṣyati grahaṇī jantoragnisādanahetubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.167"> atisāre nivṛtte 'pi mandāgnerahitāśinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhūyaḥ saṃdūṣito vahnirgrahaṇīmabhidūṣayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.168"> tasmāt kāryaḥ parīhārastvatīsāre viriktavat |
            <caesura/>
             yāvan na prakṛtisthaḥ syāddoṣataḥ prāṇatas tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.169"> ṣaṣṭhī pittadharā nāma yā kalā parikīrtitā |
            <caesura/>
             pakvāmāśayamadhyasthā grahaṇī sā prakīrtitā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.170"> grahaṇyā balamagnirhi sa cāpi grahaṇīṃ śritaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasmāt saṃdūṣite vahnau grahaṇī saṃpraduṣyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.171"> ekaśaḥ sarvaśaś caiva doṣairatyarthamucchritaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sā duṣṭā bahuśo bhuktamāmam eva vimuñcati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.172"> pakvaṃ vā sarujaṃ pūti muhurbaddhaṃ muhurdravam |
            <caesura/>
             grahaṇīrogamāhustamāyurvedavido janāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.173"> tasyotpattau vidāho+āne sadanālasyatṛṭklamāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             balakṣayo 'ruciḥ kāsaḥ karṇakṣveḍo 'ntrakūjanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.174"> atha jāte bhavejjantuḥ śūnapādakaraḥ kṛśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             parvaruglaulyatṛṭchardijvarārocakadāhavām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.175"> udgirec chuktatiktāmlalohadhūmāmagandhikam |
            <caesura/>
             prasekamukhavairasyatamakārucipīḍitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.176"> vātācchūlādhikaiḥ pāyuhṛtpārśvodaramastakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pittāt sadāhairgurubhiḥ kaphāt tribhyas trilakṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.177"> doṣavarṇair nakhais tadvad viṇmūtranayanānanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hṛtpāṇḍūdaragulmārśaḥplīhāśaṅkhī ca mānavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.178"> yathā doṣocchrayaṃ tasya viśuddhasya yathākramam |
            <caesura/>
             peyādiṃ vitaret samyag dīpanīyopasaṃbhṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.179"> tataḥ pācanasaṃgrāhidīpanīyagaṇatrayam |
            <caesura/>
             pibet prātaḥ surāriṣṭasnehamūtrasukhāmbubhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.180"> takreṇa vātha takraṃ vā kevalaṃ hitam ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             kṛmigulmodarārśoghnīḥ kriyāś cātrāvacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.181"> cūrṇaṃ hiṅgvādikaṃ cātra ghṛtaṃ vā plīhanāśanam |
            <caesura/>
             kalkena magadhādeś ca cāṅgerīsvarasena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.182ab"> caturguṇena dadhnā ca ghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ hitaṃ bhavet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.182cd"> jvarādīn avirodhāc ca sādhayet svaiś cikitsitaiḥ
            ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.40.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate
            kāyacikitsātantre 'tisārapratiṣedho nāma (dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ/)
            catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||40 ||</l>

        <div n="41" type="adhyāya">

          <head>ekacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.1"> athātaḥ śoṣapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.3"> anekarogānugato bahurogapurogamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             durvijñeyo durnivāraḥ śoṣo vyādhirmahābalaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.4"> saṃśoṣaṇādrasādīnāṃ śoṣa ity abhidhīyate |
            <caesura/>
             kriyākṣayakaratvāc ca kṣaya ity ucyate punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.5"> rājñaś candramaso yasmād abhūd eṣa kilāmayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasmāt taṃ rājayakṣmeti kecidāhuḥ punarjanāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.6"> sa vyastair jāyate doṣair iti kecid vadanti hi |
            <caesura/>
             ekādaśānām ekasmin sānnidhyāt tantrayuktitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.7"> kriyāṇām avibhāgena prāgekotpādanena ca |
            <caesura/>
             eka eva mataḥ śoṣaḥ sannipātātmako hy ataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.8"> udrekāttatra liṅgāni doṣāṇāṃ nipatanti hi |
            <caesura/>
             ksayādvegapratīghātādāghātādviṣamāśanāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.9"> jāyate kupitairdoṣairvyāptadehasya dehinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaphapradhānairdoṣairhi ruddheṣu rasavartmasu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.10"> ativyavāyino vāpi kṣīṇe retasyanantaram |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīyante dhātavaḥ sarve tataḥ śuṣyanti mānavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.11"> bhaktadveṣo jvaraḥ śvāsaḥ kāsaḥ śoṇitadarśanam |
            <caesura/>
             svarabhedaś ca jāyeta ṣaḍrūpe rājayakṣmaṇi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.12"> svarabhedo 'nilāñchūlaṃ saṃlocaś cāṃsapārśvayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jvaro dāho 'tisāraś ca pittādraktasya cāgamaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.13"> śirasaḥ paripūrṇatvamabhaktacchanda eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             kāsaḥ kaṇṭhasya coddhvaṃso vijñeyaḥ kaphakopataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.14"> ekādaśabhir ebhir vā ṣaḍbhir vāpi samanvitam |
            <caesura/>
             (kāsātīsārapārśvārtisvarabhedārucijvaraiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.15"> tribhir vā pīḍitaṃ liṅgairjvarakāsāsṛgāmayaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ) jahyācchoṣārditaṃ jantumicchan suvipulaṃ yaśaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.16"> vyāyaśokasthāviryavyāyāmadhvopavāsataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇoraḥkṣatapīḍābhyāṃ śoṣānanye vadanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.17"> vyavāyaśoṣī śukrasya kṣayaliṅgair upadrutaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pāṇḍudeho yathāpūrvaṃ kṣīyante cāsya dhātavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.18"> pradhyānaśīlaḥ srastāṅgaḥ śokaśoṣyapi tādṛśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vinā śukraksayakṛtairvikārairabhilakṣitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.19"> jarāśoṣī kṛśo mandavīryabuddhibalendiryaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kampano 'rucimān bhinnakāṃsyapātrahatasvaraḥ(naḥ) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.20"> ṣṭhīvati śleṣmaṇā hīnaṃ gauravārucipīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saṃprasrutāsyanāsākṣaḥ suptarūkṣamalacchaviḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.21"> adhvapraśoṣī srastāṅgaḥ saṃbhṛṣṭaparuṣacchaviḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prasuptagātrāvayavaḥ śuṣkaklomagalānanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.22"> vyāyāmaśoṣī bhūyiṣṭhamebhir eva samanvitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             uraḥkṣatakṛtairliṅgaiḥ saṃyuktaś ca kṣatādvinā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.23"> raktakṣayād vedanābhis tathaivāhārayantraṇāt |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇitasya bhavec choṣaḥ sa cāsādhyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.24"> vyāyāmabhārādhyayanair abhighātātimaithunaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             karmaṇā cāpy urasyena vakṣo yasya vidāritam |
            <caesura/>
             tasyor asi kṣate raktaṃ pūyaḥ śleṣmā ca gacchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.25"> kāsamānaś chardayec ca pītaraktāsitāruṇam |
            <caesura/>
             saṃtaptavakṣāḥ so 'tyarthaṃ dūyanātparitāmyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.26"> durgandhavadanocchvāso bhinnavarṇasvaro naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             keṣāṃcidevaṃ śoṣo hi kāraṇairbhedamāgataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.27"> na tatra doṣaliṅgānāṃ samastānāṃ nipātanam |
            <caesura/>
             kṣayā eva hi te jñeyāḥ pratyekaṃ dhātusaṃjñitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.28"> cikitsitaṃ tu teṣāṃ hi prāguktaṃ dhātusaṃkṣaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.29">
            śvāsāṅgasādakaphasaṃsravatāluśoṣacchardyagnisādamadapīnasapāṇḍunidrāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śoṣe bhaviṣyati bhavanti sa cāpi jantuḥ śuklekṣaṇe bhavati māṃsaparo ririṃsuḥ
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.30"> svapneṣu kākaśukaśallakinīlakaṇṭhagṛdhrās tathaiva
            kapayaḥ kṛkalāsakāś ca |
            <caesura/>
             taṃ vāhayanti sa nadīrvijalāś ca paśyec chuṣkāṃstarūn pavanadhūmadavārditāṃś
            ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.31"> mahāśanaṃ kṣīyamāṇamatīsāranipīḍitam |
            <caesura/>
             śūnamuṣkodaraṃ caiva yakṣmiṇaṃ parivarjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.32"> upācaredātmavantaṃ dīptāgnimakṛśaṃ navam |
            <caesura/>
             sthirādivargasiddhena dhṛtenājāvikena ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.33"> snigdhasya mṛdu kartavyamūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca śodhanam |
            <caesura/>
             āsthāpanaṃ tathā kāryaṃ śirasaś ca virecanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.34"> yavagodhūmaśālīṃś ca rasairbhuñjīta śodhitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dṛḍhe 'gnau bṛṃhayec cāpi nivṛttopadravaṃ naram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.35"> vyavāyaśoṣiṇaṃ prāyo bhajante vātajā gadāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bṛṃhaṇīyo vidhistasmai hitaḥ snighdo 'nilāpahaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.36"> kākānulūkānnakulān biḍālān gaṇḍūpadān vyālabileśayākhūn
            |
            <caesura/>
             gṛdhrāṃś ca dadyādvividhaiḥ pravādaiḥ sasaindhavān sarṣapatailabhṛṣṭān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.37"> deyāni māṃsāni ca jāṅgalāni mudgāḍhakīsūparasāś ca
            hṛdyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kharoṣṭranāgāśvatarāśvajāni deyāni māṃsāni sukalpitāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.38"> māṃsopadaṃśāṃś ca pibedariṣṭān mārdvīkayuktān madirāś ca
            sevyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             arkāmṛtākṣārajaloṣitebhyaḥ kṛtvā yavebhyo vividhāṃś ca bhakṣyān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.39"> khādet pibet sarpirajāvikaṃ vā kṛśo yavāgvā saha
            bhaktakāle |
            <caesura/>
             sarpirmadhubhyāṃ trikaṭu pralihyāc cavyāviḍaṅgopahitaṃ kṣayārtaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.40"> māṃsādamāṃseṣu ghṛtaṃ ca siddhaṃ śosāpahaṃ
            kṣaudrakaṇāsametam |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāsitāmāgadhikāvalehaḥ sakṣaudratailaḥ kṣayarogaghātī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.41"> ghṛtena cājena samākṣikeṇa turaṅgagandhātilamāṣacūrṇam |
            <caesura/>
             sitāśvagandhāmagadhodbhavānāṃ cūrṇaṃ ghṛtakṣaudrayutaṃ pralihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.42"> kṣīraṃ pibed vāpy atha vājigandhāvipakvamevaṃ labhate
            'ṅgapuṣṭim |
            <caesura/>
             tad utthitaṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ sitāḍhyaṃ prātaḥ pibed vāpi payonupānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.43"> utsādane cāpi turaṅgagandhā yojyā yavāś caiva punarnave
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             kṛtsne vṛṣe tatkusumaiś ca siddhaṃ sarpiḥ pibet kṣaudrayutaṃ hitāśī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.44"> yakṣmāṇam etat prabalaṃ ca kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ ca hanyād api
            pāṇḍutāṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             śakṛdrasā gośvagajāvyajānāṃ kvāthā mitāś cāpi tathaiva bhāgaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.45"> mūrvāharidrākhadiradrumāṇāṃ kṣīrasya bhāgastvaparo
            ghṛtasya |
            <caesura/>
             bhāgān daśautān vipacedvidhijño dattvā trivargaṃ madhuraṃ ca kṛtsnam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.46"> kaṭutrikaṃ caiva sabhadradāru ghṛtottamaṃ
            yakṣmanivāraṇāya |
            <caesura/>
             dve pañcamūlyau varuṇaṃ karañjaṃ bhallātakaṃ bilvapunarnave ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.47"> yavān kulatthān badarāṇi bhārgīṃ pāṭhāṃ hutāśaṃ
            samahīkadambam |
            <caesura/>
             kṛtvā kaṣāyaṃ vipaceddhi tasya ṣaḍbhir hi pātrairghṛtapātramekam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.48"> vyoṣaṃ mahāvṛkṣapayo 'bhayāṃ ca cavyaṃ surākhyaṃ
            lavaṇottamaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             etad dhi śoṣaṃ jaṭharāṇi caiva hanyāt pramehāṃś ca sahānilena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.49"> gośvāvyajebhaiṇakharoṣṭrajātaiḥ
            śakṛdrasakṣīrarasakṣatotthaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāśvagandhāmagadhāsitābhiḥ siddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ yakṣmavikārahāri || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.50"> elājamodāmalakābhayākṣagāyatryariṣṭāsanaśālasārān |
            <caesura/>
             viḍaṅgabhallātakacitrakogrākaṭutrikāmbhodasurāṣṭrajāṃś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.51"> paktvā jale tena paceddhi sarpistasmin susiddhe
            tvavatārite ca |
            <caesura/>
             triṃśatpalānyatra sitopalāyā dattvā tugākṣīripalāni ṣaṭ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.52"> prasthe ghṛtasya dviguṇaṃ ca dadyāt kṣaudraṃ tato
            manthahataṃ vidadhyāt |
            <caesura/>
             palaṃ palaṃ prātarataḥ pralihya paścāt pibet kṣīramatandritaś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.53"> etad dhi medhyaṃ paramaṃ pavitraṃ cakṣuṣyamāyuṣyamatho
            yaśasyam |
            <caesura/>
             yakṣmāṇamāśu vyapahanti caitat pāṇḍvāmayaṃ caiva bhagandaraṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.54"> śvāsaṃ ca hanti svarabhedakāsahṛtplīhagulmagrahaṇīgadāṃś
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             na cātra kiṃcit parivarjanīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ caitadupāsyamānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.55"> plīhodaroktaṃ vihitaṃ ca sarpistrīṇyeva cānyāni hitāni
            cātra |
            <caesura/>
             upadravāṃś ca svaravaikṛtādīn jayed yathāsvaṃ prasamīkṣya śāstram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.56"> ajāśakṛnmūtrapayoghṛtāsṛṅmāṃsālayāni pratisevamānaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             snānādinānāvidhinā jahāti māsādaśeṣaṃ niyamena śoṣam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.57"> rasonayogaṃ vidhivat kṣayārtaḥ kṣīreṇa vā
            nāgabalāprayogam |
            <caesura/>
             seveta vā māgadhikāvidhānaṃ tathopayogaṃ jatuno 'śmajasya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.58"> śokaṃ striyaṃ krodhamasūyanaṃ ca tyajedudārān viṣayān
            bhajeta |
            <caesura/>
             vaidyān dvijātīṃstridaśān gurūś ca vācaś ca puṇyāḥ śṛṇuyādbijebhyaḥ ||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.41.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate
            kāyacikitsātantre (tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ, ādita) ekacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||41 ||</l>

        <div n="42" type="adhyāya">
          <head>dvicatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.1"> athāto gulmapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.3"> yathoktaiḥ kopanairdoṣāḥ kupitāḥ koṣṭhamāgatāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             janayanti nṛṇāṃ gulmaṃ sa pañcavidha ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.4"> hṛdbastyor antare granthiḥ saṃcārī yadi vācalaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             cayāpacayavān vṛttaḥ sa gulma iti kīrtitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.5ab"> pañca gulmāśrayā nṝṇāṃ pārśve hṛnnābhibastayaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.5cd">gupitānilamūlatvād gūḍhamūlodayād api || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.6ab"> gulmavad vā viśālatvād gulma ity abhidhīyate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.6cd">sa yasmād ātmani cayaṃ gacchaty apsv iva budbudaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.7"> antaḥ sarati yasmāc ca na pākam upayātyataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sa vyastair jāyate doṣaiḥ samastair api cocchritaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.8"> puruṣāṇāṃ tathā strīṇāṃ jñeyo raktena cāparaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sadanaṃ madantā vahner āṭopo 'ntravikūjanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.9ab"> viṇmūtrānilasaṅgaś ca sauhityās ahatā tathā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.9cd"> dveṣo 'nne vāyurūrdhvaṃ ca pūrvarūpeṣu gulminām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.10"> hṛtkukṣiśūlaṃ mukhakaṇṭhaśoṣo vāyor nirodho viṣamāgnitā
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             te te vikārāḥ pavanātmakāś ca bhavanti gulme 'nilasaṃbhave tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.11"> svedajvarāhāravidāhadāhāstṛṣṇāṅgarāgaḥ kaṭuvaktratā ca |
            <caesura/>
             pittasya liṅgānyakhilāni yāni pittātmake tāni bhavanti gulme || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.12"> staimity am anne 'ruciraṅgasādaś chardiḥ praseko
            madhurāsyatā ca |
            <caesura/>
             kaphasya liṅgāni ca yāni tāni bhavanti gulme kaphasaṃbhave tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.13"> sarvātmakaḥ sarvavikārayuktaḥ so 'sādhya uktaḥ kṣatajaṃ
            pravakṣye |
            <caesura/>
             navaprasūtāhitabhojanā yā yā cāmagarbhaṃ visṛjedṛtau vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.14"> vāyur hi tasyāḥ parigṛhya raktaṃ karoti gulmaṃ sarujaṃ
            sadāham |
            <caesura/>
             paittasya liṅgena samānaliṅgaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ cāpy aparaṃ nibodha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.15"> na spandate nodarameti vṛddhiṃ bhavanti liṅgāni ca
            garbhiṇīnām |
            <caesura/>
             taṃ garbhakālātigame caikitsyamasṛgbhavaṃ gulmamuśanti tajjñāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.16"> vātagulmārditaṃ snigdhaṃ yuktaṃ snehavirecanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             upācared yathākālaṃ nirūhaiḥ sānuvāsanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.17"> pittagulmārditaṃ snigdhaṃ kākolyādighṛtena tu |
            <caesura/>
             viriktaṃ madhurairyogairnirūhaiḥ samupācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.18"> śleṣmagulmārditaṃ snigdhaṃ pippalyādighṛtena tu |
            <caesura/>
             tīkṣṇairviriktaṃ tad rūpairnirūhaiḥ samupācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.19"> sannipātotthite gulme tridoṣaghno vidhirhitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pittavadraktagulminyā nāryāḥ kāryaḥ kriyāvidhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.20"> viśeṣamaparaṃ cāsyāḥ śṛṇu raktavibhedanam |
            <caesura/>
             palāśakṣāratoyena siddhaṃ sarpiḥ prayojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.21ab"> dadyād uttarabastiṃ ca pippalyādighṛtena tu | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.21cd"> uṣṇair vā bhedayed bhinne vidhirāsṛgdaro hitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.22"> ānūpaudakamajjāno vasā tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ dadhi |
            <caesura/>
             vipakvam ekataḥ śastaṃ vātagulme 'nuvāsanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.23"> jāṅgalaikaśaphānāṃ tu vasā sarpiś ca paittike |
            <caesura/>
             tailaṃ jāṅgalamajjāna evaṃ gulme kaphotthite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.24"> dhātrīphalānāṃ svarase ṣaḍaṅgaṃ vipaced ghṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             śarkarāsaindhavopetaṃ tad dhitaṃ vātagulmine || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.25"> citrakavyoṣasindhūtthapṛthvīkācavyadāḍimaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dīpyakagranthikājājīhapuṣādhānyakaiḥ samaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.26"> dadhyāranālabadaramūlakasvarasairghṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             tatpibedvātagulmāgnidaurbalyāṭopaśūlanut || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.27"> hiṅgusauvarcalājājīviḍadāḍimadīpyakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             puṣkaravyoṣadhānyāmlavetasakṣāracitrakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.28"> śaṭīvacājagandhailāsurasaiś ca vipācitam |
            <caesura/>
             śūlānāhaharaṃ sarpirdadhnā cānilagulminām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.29"> viḍadāḍimasindhūtthahutabhugvyoṣajīrakaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hiṅgusauvarcalakṣārarugvṛkṣāmlāmlavetasaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.30"> bījapūrarasopetaṃ sarpirdadhicaturguṇam |
            <caesura/>
             sādhitṃ dādhikaṃ nāma gulmahṛt plīhaśūlajit || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.31"> rasonasvarase sarpiḥ pañcamūlarasānvitam |
            <caesura/>
             surāranāladadhyamlamūlakasvarasaiḥ saha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.32"> vyoṣadāḍimavṛkṣāmlayavānīcavyasaindhavaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hiṅgvamlavetasājājīdīpyakaiś ca samāṃśikaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.33"> siddhaṃ gulmagrahaṇyarśaḥśvāsonmādakṣayajvarān |
            <caesura/>
             kāsāpasmāramandāgniplīhaśūlānilāñjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.34"> dadhi sauvīrakaṃ sarpiḥ kvāthau mudgakulatthajau |
            <caesura/>
             pañcāḍhakāni vipaced āvāpya dvipalāny atha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.35"> sauvarcalaṃ sarjikāṃ ca devadārv atha saindhavam |
            <caesura/>
             vātagulmāpahaṃ sarpir etad dīpanam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.36"> tṛṇamūlakaṣāye tu jīvanīyaiḥ pacedghṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             nyagrodhādigaṇe vāpi gaṇe vāpy utpalādike || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.37"> raktapittotthitaṃ ghnanti ghṛtāny etāny asaṃśayam |
            <caesura/>
             āragvadhādau vipaceddīpanīyayutaṃ ghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.38"> kṣāravarge pacec cānyat pacen mūtragaṇe 'param |
            <caesura/>
             ghnanti gulmaṃ kaphodbhūtaṃ ghṛtānyetānyasaṃśayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.39"> yathādoṣocchrayaṃ cāpi cikitsetsānnipātikam |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇaṃ hiṅgvādikaṃ vāpi ghṛtaṃ vā plīhanāśanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.40"> pibed gulmāpahaṃ kāle sarpistailvakam eva vā |
            <caesura/>
             tilekṣurakapālāśasārṣapaṃ yāvanālajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.41"> bhasma mūlakajaṃ cāpi gojāvikharahantinām |
            <caesura/>
             mūtreṇa mahiṣīṇāṃ ca pālikaiś cāvacūrṇitaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.42"> kuṣṭhasaindhavayaṣṭyāhvanāgarakṛmighātibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sājamodaiś ca daśabhiḥ sāmudrāc ca palairyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.43"> ayaḥpātre 'gninālpena paktvā lehyam(laham) athoddharet |
            <caesura/>
             tasya mātrāṃ pibed dadhnā surayā sarpiṣāpi vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.44"> dhānyāmlenoṣṇatoyena kaulatthena rasena vā |
            <caesura/>
             gulmān vātavikārāṃś ca kṣāro 'yaṃ hantyasaṃśayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.45"> svarjikākuṣṭhasahitaḥ kṣāraḥ ketakijo 'pi vā |
            <caesura/>
             tailena śamayet pīto gulmaṃ pavanasaṃbhavam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.46"> pītaṃ sukhāmbunā vāpi svarjikākuṣṭhasaindhavam |
            <caesura/>
             vṛś cīvamurubūkaṃ(vṛś cīramurubūkaṃ) ca varṣābhūrbṛhatīdvayam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.47"> citrakaṃ ca jaladroṇe paktvā pādāvaśeṣitam |
            <caesura/>
             māgadhīciktrakakṣaudralipte kumbhe nidhāpayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.48"> madhunaḥ prasthamāvāpya pathyācūrṇārdhasaṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             busoṣitaṃ daśāhaṃ tu jīrṇabhaktaḥ piben naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.49"> ariṣṭo 'yaṃ jayed gulmamavipākamarocakam |
            <caesura/>
             pāṭhānikumbharajanītrikaṭutriphalāgnikam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.50"> lavaṇaṃ vṛkṣabījaṃ ca tulyaṃ syād anavo guḍaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pathyābhir vā yutaṃ cūrṇaṃ gavāṃ mūtrayutaṃ pacet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.51"> guṭikāstadghṛnībhūtaṃ kṛtvā khādedabhuktavān |
            <caesura/>
             gulmaplīhāgnisādāṃtā nāśayeyuraśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.52"> hṛdrogaṃ grahaṇīdoṣaṃ pāṇḍurogaṃ ca dāruṇam |
            <caesura/>
             saśūle sonnate 'spande dāhapākaruganvite || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.53ab"> gulme raktaṃ jalaukobhiḥ sirāmokṣeṇa vā haret |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.53cd"> sukhoṣṇā jāṅgalarasāḥ susnigdhā vyaktasaindhavāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.54ab"> kaṭutrikasamāyuktā hitāḥ pāne tu gulminām |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.54cd"> peyā vātaharaiḥ siddhāḥ kaulatthāḥ saṃskṛtā rasāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.55"> khalāḥ sapañcamūlāś ca gulmināṃ bhojane hitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             baddhavarconilānāṃ tu sārdrakaṃ kṣīramiṣyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.56"> kumbhīpiṇḍeṣṭakāsvedān kārayet kuśalo bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             gulminaḥ sarva evoktā durvirecyatamā bhṛśam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.57"> ataśaitāṃs tu susvinnān sraṃsanenopapādayet |
            <caesura/>
             vimlāpanābhyañjanāni tathaiva dahanāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.58"> upanāhāś ca kartavyāḥ sukhoṣṇāḥ sālvaṇādayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             udaroktāni sarpīṃṣi mūtravartikriyās tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.59"> lavaṇāni ca yojyāni yānyuktānyanilāmaye |
            <caesura/>
             vātavarconirodhe tu sāmudrārdrakasarṣapaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.60"> kṛtvā pāyau vidhātavyā vartayo maricottarāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dantīcitrakamūleṣu tathā vātahareṣu ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.61"> kuryād ariṣṭān sarvāṃś ca ślokasthāne yatheritān |
            <caesura/>
             khādedvāpyaṅkurān bhṛṣṭān pūtīkanṛpavṛkṣayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.62"> ūrdhvavātaṃ manuṣyaṃ ca gulminaṃ na nirūhayet |
            <caesura/>
             pibettrivṛnnāgaraṃ vā saguḍāṃ vā harītakīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.63"> gugguluṃ trivṛtāṃ dantīṃ dravantīṃ saindhavaṃ vacām |
            <caesura/>
             mūtramadyapayodrākṣārasairvīkṣya balābalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.64"> evaṃ pīlūni bhṛṣṭāni pibet salavaṇāni tu |
            <caesura/>
             pippalīpippalīmūlacavyacitrakasaindhavaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.65"> yuktā hanti surā gulmaṃ śīghraṃ kāle prayojitā |
            <caesura/>
             baddhaviṇmāruto gulmī bhuñjīta payasā yavān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.66"> kulmāṣān vā bahusnehān bhakṣyellavaṇottarān |
            <caesura/>
             athāsyopadravaḥ śūlaḥ kathaṃcid upajāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.67"> śūlaṃ nikhānitamivāsukhaṃ yena tu vattyasau |
            <caesura/>
             tatra viṇmūtrasaṃrodhaḥ kṛcchrocchvāsaḥ sthirāṅgatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.68"> tṛṣṇā dāho bhramo 'nnasya vidagdhaparivṛddhitā |
            <caesura/>
             romaharṣo 'ruciś chardir bhuktavṛddhir jaḍāṅgatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.69"> vāyvādibhir yathāsaṅkhyāṃ miśrair vā vīkṣya yojayet |
            <caesura/>
             pathyātrilavaṇaṃ kṣāraṃ hiṅgutumburupauṣkaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.70"> yavānīṃ ca haridrāṃ ca viḍaṅgānyamlavetasam |
            <caesura/>
             vidārītriphalābhīruśṛṅgāṭīguḍaśarkarāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.71"> kāśmarīphalayaṣṭyāhvaparūṣakahimāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             ṣaḍgranthātiviṣādārupathyāmaricavṛkṣajān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.72"> kṛṣṇāmūlakacanvyaṃ ca nāgarakṣāracitrakān |
            <caesura/>
             uṣṇāmlakāñjikakṣīratoyaiḥ ślokasamāpanān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.73"> yathākramaṃ vimiśrāṃś ca dvandve sarvāṃś ca sarvaje |
            <caesura/>
             tathaiva sekāvagāhapradehābhyaṅgabhojanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.74"> śiśirodakapūrṇānāṃ bhājanānāṃ ca dhāraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             vamanonmardanasvedalaṅghanakṣapaṇakriyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.75"> snehādiś ca karamaḥ sarvo viśeṣeṇopadiśyate |
            <caesura/>
             vallūraṃ mūlakaṃ matsyān śuṣkaśākāni vaidalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.76"> na khādedālukaṃ gulmī madhurāṇi phalāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             vinā gulmena yacchūlaṃ gulmasthāneṣu jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.77"> nidānaṃ tasya vakṣyāmi rūpaṃ ca sacikitsitam |
            <caesura/>
             vātamūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ nigrahādatibhojanāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.78"> ajīrṇādhyaśanāyāsaviruddhānnopasevanāt |
            <caesura/>
             pānīyapānāt kṣutkāle virūḍhānāṃ ca sevanāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.79"> piṣṭānnaśuṣkamāṃsānām upayogāttathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             evaṃvidhānāṃ dravyāṇāmanyeṣāṃ copasevanāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.80"> vāyuḥ prakupitaḥ koṣṭhe śūlaṃ saṃjanayed bhṛśam |
            <caesura/>
             nirucchvāsī bhavettena vedanāpīḍito naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.81"> śaṅkusphoṭanavattasya yasmāttīvrāś ca vedanāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śūlāsaktasya lakṣyante tasmācchūlamihocyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.82"> nirāhārasya yasyaiva tīvraṃ śūlamudīryate |
            <caesura/>
             prastabdhagātro bhavati kṛcchreṇocchvasitīva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.83"> vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi kṛcchreṇa kurute naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             etairliṅgairvijānīyācchūlaṃ vātasamudbhavam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.84"> tṛṣṇā dāho mado mūrcchā tīvraṃ śūlaṃ tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             śītābhikāmo bhavati śītenaiva praśāmyati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.85"> etairliṅgairvijānīyācchūlaṃ pittasamudbhavam |
            <caesura/>
             śūlenotpīḍyamānasya hṛllāsa upajāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.86"> atīva pūrṇakoṣṭhatvaṃ tathaiva gurugātratā |
            <caesura/>
             etacchleṣmasamutthasya śūlasyoktaṃ nidarśanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.87"> sarvāṇi dṛṣṭvā rūpāṇi nirdiśetsānnipātikam |
            <caesura/>
             sannipātasamutthānamasādhyaṃ taṃ vinirdiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.88"> śūlānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ cikitsāṃ tu nibodha me |
            <caesura/>
             āśukārī hi pavanastasmāt taṃ tvarayā jayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.89"> tasya śūlābhipannasya sveda eva sukhāvahaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pāyasaiḥ kṛśarāpiṇḍaiḥ snigdhair vā piśitairhitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.90"> trivṛcchākena vā snigdhamuṣṇaṃ bhiñjīta bhojanam |
            <caesura/>
             cirabilvāṅkurān vāpi tailabhṛṣṭāṃs tu bhakṣayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.91"> vaihaṅgāṃś ca rasān snigdhān jāṅgalān śūlapīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathālābhaṃ niṣeveta māṃsāni bilaśāyinām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.92"> surā sauvīrakaṃ cukraṃ mastūdaśvittathā dadhi |
            <caesura/>
             sakālalavaṇaṃ peyaṃ śūle vātasamudbhave || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.93"> kulatthayūṣo yuktāmlo lāvakīyūṣasaṃskṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sasaindhavaḥ samarico vātaśūlavināśanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.94"> viḍaṅgaśigrukampillapathyāśyāmāmlavetasān |
            <caesura/>
             surasāmaśvamūtrīṃ ca sauvarcalayutān pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.95"> madyena vātajaṃ śūlaṃ kṣipram eva praśāmyati |
            <caesura/>
             pṛthvīkājājicavikāyavānīvyoṣacitrakāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.96"> pippalyaḥ pippalīmūlaṃ saindhavaṃ ceti cūrṇayet |
            <caesura/>
             tāni cūrṇāni payasā pibet kāmbalikena vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.97"> madhvāsavena cukreṇa surāsauvīrakeṇa vā |
            <caesura/>
             athavaitāni(athacaitāni) cūrṇāni mātuluṅgarasena vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.98"> tathā badarayūṣeṇa bhāvitāni punaḥ punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tāni hiṅgupragāḍhāni saha śarkarayā pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.99"> saha dāḍimasāreṇa vartiḥ kāryā bhiṣagjitā |
            <caesura/>
             sā vartirvātikaṃ śūlaṃ kṣipram eva vyapohati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.100"> guḍatailena vā līḍhā pītā madyena vā punaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bubhukṣāprabhave śūle laghu saṃtarpaṇaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.101"> uṣṇaiḥ kṣīrairyavāgūbhiḥ snigdhairmāṃsarasais tathā |
            <caesura/>
             vātaśūle samutpanne rūkṣaṃ snigdhena bhojayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.102"> susaṃskṛtāḥ pradeyāḥ syurghṛtapūrā viśeṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vāruṇīṃ ca pibejjantus tathā saṃpadyate sukhī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.103"> etadvātasamutthasya śūlasyoktaṃ cikitsitam |
            <caesura/>
             atha pittasamutthasya kriyāṃ vakṣyāmyataḥ param || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.104"> sa sukhaṃ chardayitvā tu pītvā śītodakaṃ naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śītalāni ca seveta sarvāṇyuṣṇāni varjayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.105"> maṇirājatatāmrāṇi bhājanāni ca sarvaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vāripūrṇāni tānyasya śūlasyopari nikṣipet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.106"> guḍaḥ śāliryavāḥ kṣīraṃ sarpiḥpānaṃ virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             jāṅgalāni ca māṃsāni bheṣajaṃ pittaśūlinām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.107"> rasān seveta pittaghnān pittalāni vivarjayet |
            <caesura/>
             pālāśaṃ dhānvanaṃ vāpi pibedyūṣaṃ saśarkaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.108"> parūṣakāṇi mṛdvīkākharjūrodakajānyapi |
            <caesura/>
             tat pibec charkarāyuktaṃ pittaśūlanivāraṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.109"> aśane bhuktamātre tu prakopaḥ ślaiṣmikasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             vamanaṃ kārayettatra pippalīvāriṇā bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.110"> rūkṣaḥ svedaḥ prayojyaḥ syād anyāś coṣṇāḥ kriyā hitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pippalī śṛṅgaveraṃ ca śleṣmaśūle bhiṣagjitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.111"> pāṭhāṃ vacāṃ trikaṭukaṃ tathā kaṭukarohiṇīm |
            <caesura/>
             citrakasya ca niryūhe pibedyūṣaṃ sahārjakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.112"> eraṇḍaphalamūlāni mūlaṃ gokṣurakasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             śālaparṇīṃ pṛśniparṇīṃ bṛhatīṃ kaṇṭakārikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.113"> dadyācchṛgālavinnāṃ ca sahadevāṃ tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             mahāsahāṃ kṣudrasahāṃ mūlamikṣurakasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.114"> etat saṃbhṛtya saṃbhāraṃ jaladroṇe vipācayet |
            <caesura/>
             caturbhāgāvaśeṣaṃ tu yavakṣārayutaṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.115"> vātikaṃ paittikaṃ vāpi ślaiṣmikaṃ sānnipātikam |
            <caesura/>
             prasahya nāśayec chūlaṃ chinnābhram iva mārutaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.116"> pippalī svarjikākṣāro yavāś citraka eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             sevyaṃ caitat samānīya bhasma kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.117"> tad uṣṇavāriṇā pītaṃ śleṣmaśūle bhiṣagjitam |
            <caesura/>
             ruṇaddhi mārutaṃ śleṣmā kukṣipārśvavyavasthitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.118"> sa saṃruddhaḥ karotyāśu sādhmānaṃ guḍguḍāyanam |
            <caesura/>
             sūcībhir iva nistodaṃ kṛcchrocchvāsī tadā naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.119"> nānnaṃ vāñchati no nidrām upaity artinipīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pārśvaśūlaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ kaphānilasamudbhavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.120"> tatra puṣkaramūlāni hiṅgu sauvarcalaṃ viḍam |
            <caesura/>
             saindhavaṃ tumburuṃ pathyāṃ cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā tu pāyayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.121"> pārśvahṛdbastiśūleṣu yavakvāthena saṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             sarpiḥ plīhodaroktaṃ vā ghṛtaṃ vā hiṅgusaṃyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.122"> bījapūrakasāraṃ vā payasā saha sādhitam |
            <caesura/>
             eraṇḍatailamathavā madyamas tu payorasaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.123"> bhojayec cāpi payasā jāṅgalena rasena vā |
            <caesura/>
             prakupyati yadā kukṣau vahnimākramya mārutaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.124"> tadāsya bhojanaṃ bhuktaṃ sopastambhaṃ na pacyate |
            <caesura/>
             ucchvasity āmaśakṛtā śūlenāhanyate muhuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.125"> naivāsane na śayane tiṣṭhan vā labhate sukham |
            <caesura/>
             kukṣiśūla iti khyāto vātādāmasamudbhavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.126"> vamanaṃ kārayettatra laṅghayed vā yathābalam |
            <caesura/>
             saṃsargapācanaṃ kuryād amlair dīpanasaṃyutaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.127"> nāgaraṃ dīpyakaṃ cavyaṃ hiṅgu sauvarcalaṃ viḍam |
            <caesura/>
             mātuluṅgasya bījāni tathā śyāmorubūkayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.128"> bṛhatyāḥ kaṇṭakāryāś ca kvāthaṃ śūlaharaṃ pibet |
            <caesura/>
             vacā sauvarcalaṃ hiṅgu kuṣṭhaṃ sātiviṣābhayā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.129"> kuṭajasya ca bījāni sadyaḥśūlaharāṇi tu |
            <caesura/>
             virecane prayuñjīta jñātvā doṣabalābalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.130"> snehabastīn nirūhāṃś ca kuryād doṣanibarhaṇān |
            <caesura/>
             upanāhāḥ snehasekā dhānyāmlapariṣecanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.131"> avagāhāś ca śasyante yac cānyad api tad dhitam |
            <caesura/>
             kaphapittāvaruddhas tu māruto rasamūrcchitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.132"> hṛdisthaḥ kurute śūlamucchvāsārodhakaṃ param |
            <caesura/>
             sa hṛcchūla iti khyāto rasamārutasaṃbhavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.133"> tatrāpi karmābhihitaṃ yadi uktaṃ hṛdvikāriṇām |
            <caesura/>
             saṃrodhāt kupito vāyuri bastim āvṛtya tiṣṭhati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.134"> bastivaṅkṣaṇanābhīṣu tataḥ śūlo 'sya jāyate |
            <caesura/>
             viṇmūtravātasaṃrodhī bastiśūlaḥ sa mārutāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.135"> nābhyāṃ vaṅkṣaṇapārśveṣu kukṣau meḍhrāntramardakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtramāvṛtya gṛhṇāti mūtraśūlaḥ sa mārutāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.136"> vāyuḥ prakupito yasya rūkṣāhārasya dehinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             malaṃ ruṇaddhi koṣṭhasthaṃ mandīkṛtya tu pāvakam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.137"> śūlaṃ saṃjanayaṃstīvraṃ srotāṃsyāvṛtya tasya hi |
            <caesura/>
             dakṣiṇaṃ yadi vā vāmaṃ kukṣimādāya jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.138"> sarvatra vardhate kṣipraṃ bhramannatha saghoṣavān |
            <caesura/>
             pipāsā vardhate tīvrā bhramo mūrcchā ca jāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.139"> uccārito mūtritaś ca na śāntimadhigacchati |
            <caesura/>
             viṭśūlametajjānīyādbhiṣak paramadāruṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.140"> kṣipraṃ doṣaharaṃ kāryaṃ bhiṣajā sādhu jānatā |
            <caesura/>
             svedanaṃ śamanaṃ caiva nirūhāḥ snehabastayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.141"> pūrvoddiṣṭān pāyayeta yogān koṣṭhaviśodhanān |
            <caesura/>
             udāvartaharāś cāsya kriyāḥ sarvāḥ sukhāvahāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.142"> atimātraṃ yadā bhuktaṃ pāvake mṛdutāṃ gate |
            <caesura/>
             sthirībhūtaṃ tu tatkoṣṭhe vāyurāvṛtya tiṣṭhati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.143"> avipākagataṃ hy annaṃ śūlaṃ tīvraṃ karotyati |
            <caesura/>
             mūrcchādhmānaṃ vidāhaś ca hṛdutkleśo vilambikā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.144"> viricyate chardayati kampate 'tha vimuhyati |
            <caesura/>
             avipākād bhavec chūlas tv annadoṣasamudbhavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.145"> vamanaṃ laṅghanaṃ svedaḥ pācanaṃ phalavartayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṣārāś cūrṇāni guṭikāḥ śasyante śūlanāśanāḥ ||
            <caesura/>
             gulmāvasthāḥ kriyāḥ kāryā yathāvat sarvaśūlinām ||</l>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.42.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate
            kāyacikitsātantre gulmapratiṣedho nāma (caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ)
            dvicatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||42 ||</l>
        </div>


        <div n="43" type="adhyāya">
          <head>tricatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.1"> athāto hṛdrogapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.3"> vegāghātoṣṇarūkṣānnairatimātropasevitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viruddhādhyaśanājīrṇairasātmyaiś cāpi(cāti) bhojanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.4"> dūṣayitvā rasaṃ doṣā viguṇā hṛdayaṃ gatāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kurvanti hṛdaye bādhāṃ hṛdrogaṃ taṃ pracakṣate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.5"> caturvidhaḥ sa doṣaiḥ syāt kṛmibhiś ca pṛthak pṛthak |
            <caesura/>
             lakṣaṇaṃ tasya vakṣyāmi cikitsitamanantaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.6"> āyamyate mārutaje hṛdayaṃ tudyate tathā |
            <caesura/>
             nirmathyate dīryate ca sphoṭyate pāṭyate 'pi ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.7"> tṛṣṇoṣādāhacoṣāḥ syuḥ paittike hṛdayaklamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dhūmāyanaṃ ca mūrcchā ca svedaḥ śoṣo mukhasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.8"> gauravaṃ kaphasaṃsrāvo 'ruciḥ stambho 'gnimārdavam |
            <caesura/>
             mādhuryam api cāsyasya balāsāvatate hṛdi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.9"> utkleśaḥ ṣṭhīvanaṃ todaḥ śūlo hṛllāsakastamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             aruciḥ śyāvnetratvaṃ śoṣaś ca kṛmije bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.10"> bhramaklamau sādaśoṣau jñeyās teṣām upadravāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṛmije kṛmijātīnāṃ ślaiṣmikāṇāṃ ca ye matāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.11"> vātopasṛṣṭe hṛdaye vāmayet snigdhamāturam |
            <caesura/>
             dvipañcamūlakvāthena sasnehalavaṇena tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.12"> pippalyelāvacāhiṅguyavabhasmāni saindhavam |
            <caesura/>
             sauvarcalamatho śuṇṭhīmajamodāṃ ca cūrṇitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.13"> phaladhānyāmlakaulatthadadhimadyāsavādibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pāyayeta viśuddhaṃ ca snehenānyatamena vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.14"> bhojayejjīrṇaśālyannaṃ jāṅgalaiḥ saghṛtai rasaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vātaghnasiddhaṃ tailaṃ ca dadyādbastiṃ pramāṇataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.15"> śrīparṇīmadhukakṣaudrasitotpalajalairvamet |
            <caesura/>
             pittopasṛṣṭe hṛdaye seveta madhuraiḥ śṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.16"> ghṛtaṃ kaṣāyāṃś coddiṣṭān pittajvaravināśanān |
            <caesura/>
             tṛptasya ca rasairmukhyairmadhuraiḥ saghṛtairbhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.17"> sakṣaudraṃ vitaredbastau tailaṃ madhukasādhitam |
            <caesura/>
             vacānimbakaṣāyābhyāṃ vāntaṃ hṛdi kaphātmake || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.18"> cūrṇaṃ tu pāyayetoktaṃ vātaje bhojayec ca tam |
            <caesura/>
             phalādimatha mustādiṃ triphalāṃ vā piben naraḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.19"> śyāmātrivṛtkalkayutaṃ ghṛtaṃ vāpi virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             balātailairvidadhyāc ca bastiṃ bastiviśāradaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.20"> kṛmihṛdrogiṇaṃ snigdhaṃ bhojayet piśitaudanam |
            <caesura/>
             dadhnā ca palalopetaṃ tryahaṃ paścād virecayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.21"> sugandhibhiḥ salavaṇairyogaiḥ sājājiśarkaraiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viḍaṅgagāḍhaṃ dhānyāmlaṃ pāyayetāpyanantaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.22"> hṛdayasthāḥ patantyevamadhastāt krimayo nṛṇām |
            <caesura/>
             yavānnaṃ vitareccāsya saviḍaṅgamataḥ param ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.43.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate
            kāyacikitsātantre hṛdrogapratiṣedho nāma (pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ)
            tricatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||43 ||</l>
        </div>


        <div n="44" type="adhyāya">
          <head>catuś catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.1"> athātaḥ pāṇḍurogapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvandariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.3"> vyavāyamamlaṃ lavaṇāni madyaṃ mṛdaṃ divāsvapnamatīva
            tīkṣṇam |
            <caesura/>
             niṣevamāṇasya vidūṣya raktaṃ kurvanti doṣāstvaci pāṇḍubhāvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.4"> pāṇḍvāmayo 'ṣṭārdhavidhaḥ pradiṣṭaḥ
            pṛthaksamastairyugapac ca doṣaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarveṣu caiteṣv iha pāṇḍubhāvo yato 'dhiko 'taḥ khalu pāṇḍurogaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.5"> tvaksphoṭanaṃ ṣṭhīvanagātrasādau mṛdbhakṣaṇaṃ
            prekṣaṇakūṭaśothaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viṇmūtrapītatvamathāvipāko bhaviṣyatas tasya puraḥsarāṇi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.6"> sa kāmalāpānakipāṇḍurogaḥ kumbhāhvayo
            lāgharako(lāghavako)+alasākhyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vibhāṣyate lakṣaṇamasya kṛtsnaṃ nibodha vakṣyāmyanupūrvaśastat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.7"> kṛṣṇekṣaṇaṃ kṛṣṇasirāvanaddhaṃ tadvarṇaviṇmūtranakhānanaṃ
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             vātena pāṇḍuṃ manujaṃ vyavasyed yuktaṃ tathānyais tadupadravaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.8"> pītekṣaṇaṃ pītasirāvanaddhaṃ tadvarṇaviṇmūtranakhānanaṃ
