            ca |
            <caesura/>
             pittena pāṇḍuṃ manujaṃ vyavasyed yuktaṃ tathānyais tadupadravaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.9"> śuklekṣaṇaṃ śuklasirāvanaddhaṃ tadvarṇaviṇmūtranakhānanaṃ
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             kaphena pāṇḍuṃ manujaṃ vyavasyed yuktaṃ tathānyais tadupadravaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.10"> sarvātmake sarvam idaṃvyavasyed vakṣyāmi liṅgānyatha
            kāmalāyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yo hyāmayānte sahasānnamamlamadyādapathyāni ca tasya pittam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.11"> karoti pāṇḍuṃ vadanaṃ viśeṣāt pūrveritau
            tandribalakṣayau ca |
            <caesura/>
             bhedas tu tasyāḥ khalu kumbhasāhvaḥ śopho mahāṃs tatra ca parvabhedaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.12"> jvarāṅgamardabhramasādatandrākṣayānvito
            lāgharako(lāghavako)+alasākhyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             taṃ vātapittāddharipītanīlaṃ halīmakaṃ nāma vadanti tajjñāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.13"> upadravās teṣv aruciḥ pipāsā chardirjvaro
            mūrdharujāgnisādaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śophas tathā kaṇṭhagato 'balatvaṃ mūrcchā klamo hṛdyavapīḍanaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.14"> sādhyaṃ tu pāṇḍvāmayinaṃ samīkṣya snigdhaṃ
            ghṛtenordhvamadhaś ca śuddham |
            <caesura/>
             saṃpādayet kṣaudraghṛtapragāḍhairharītakīcūrṇayutaiḥ prayogaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.15"> pibed ghṛtaṃ vā rajanīvipakvaṃ yantraiphalaṃ tailvakam
            eva vāpi |
            <caesura/>
             virecanadravyakṛtaṃ pibedvā yogāṃś ca vairecanidān ghṛtena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.16"> mūtre nikumbhārdhapalaṃ vipācya pibed abhīkṣṇaṃ
            kuḍavārdhamātram |
            <caesura/>
             khāded guḍaṃ vāpy abhayāvipakvamāragvadhādikvathitaṃ pibedvā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.17"> ayorajovyoṣaviḍaṅgacūrṇaṃ lihyād dharidrāṃ
            triphalānvitāṃ vā |
            <caesura/>
             sarpir madhubhyāṃ vidadhīta vāpi śāstrapradeśābhihitāṃś ca yogān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.18"> ahrec ca doṣān bahuśo 'lpamātrān śvayed dhi doṣeṣv
            atinirhṛteṣu |
            <caesura/>
             dhātrīphalānāṃ rasamikṣujaṃ ca manthaṃ pibet kṣaudrayutaṃ hitāśī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.19"> ubhe bṛhatyau rajanīṃ śukākhyāṃ kākādanīṃ cāpi
            sakākamācīm |
            <caesura/>
             ādāribimbīṃ sakadambapuṣpīṃ vipācya sarpirvipacet kaṣāye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.20"> tat pāṇḍutāṃ hantyupayujyamānaṃ kṣīeṇa vā māgadhikā
            yathāgni |
            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ ca yaṣṭīmadhujaṃ kaṣāyaṃ cūrṇaṃ samaṃ vā madhunāvalihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.21"> gomūtrayuktaṃ triphalādalānāṃ dattvāyasaṃ
            cūrṇamanalpakālam |
            <caesura/>
             pravālamuktāñjanaśaṅkhacūrṇaṃ lihyāttathā kāñcanagairikottham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.22"> ājaṃ śakṛtsyāt kuḍavapramāṇaṃ viḍaṃ haridrā lavaṇottamaṃ
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             pṛthak palāṃśāni samagrametaccūrṇaṃ hitāśī madhunāvalihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.23"> maṇḍūralohāgniviḍaṅgapathyāvyoṣāṃśakaḥ sarvasamānatāpyaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrāsuto 'yaṃ madhunāvalehaḥ pāṇḍvāmayaṃ hantyacireṇa ghoram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.24"> bibhītakāyomalanāgarāṇāṃ cūrṇaṃ tilānāṃ ca guḍaś ca
            mukhyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             takrānupāno vaṭakaḥ prayuktaḥ kṣiṇoti ghorānapi pāṇḍurogān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.25"> sauvarcalaṃ hiṅgu kirātatiktaṃ kalāyamātrāṇi sukhāmbunā
            vā |
            <caesura/>
             mūrvāharidrāmalakaṃ ca lihyāt sthitaṃ gavāṃ saptadināni mūtre || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.26"> mūlaṃ balācitrakayoḥ pibedvā pāṇḍvāmayārto 'kṣasamaṃ
            hitāśī |
            <caesura/>
             sukhāmbunā vā lavaṇena tulyaṃ śigroḥ phalaṃ kṣīrabhujopayojyam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.27"> nyagrodhavargasya pibet kaṣāyaṃ śītaṃ sitākṣaudrayutaṃ
            hitāśī |
            <caesura/>
             śālādikaṃ cāpy atha sāracūrṇaṃ dhātrīphalaṃ vā madhunāvalihyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.28"> viḍaṅgamustatriphalājamodaparūṣakavyoṣavinirdahanyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇāni kṛtvā guḍaśarkare ca tathaiva sarpirmadhunī śume ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.29"> saṃbhārametadvipacennidhāya sārodake sāravato gaṇasya |
            <caesura/>
             jātaṃ ca lehyaṃ matimān viditvā nidhāpayenmokṣakaje samudge || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.30"> hantyeṣa lehaḥ khalu pāṇḍurogaṃ saśothamugrām api
            kāmalāṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             saśarkarā kāmalināṃ tribhaṇḍī hitā gavākṣī saguḍā ca śuṇṭhī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.31"> kāleyake cāpi ghṛtaṃ vipakvaṃ hitaṃ ca tat syād
            rajanīvimiśram |
            <caesura/>
             dhātuṃ nadījaṃ jatu śailajaṃ vā kumbhāhvaye mūtrayutaṃ pibedvā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.32"> mūtre sthitaṃ saindhavasaṃprayuktaṃ māsaṃ pibedvāpi hi
            lohakiṭṭam |
            <caesura/>
             dagdhvākṣakāṣṭhairmalamāyasaṃ vā gomūtranirvāpitamaṣṭavārān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.33"> vicūrṇya līḍhaṃ madhunācireṇa kumbhāhvayaṃ pāṇḍugadaṃ
            nihanyāt |
            <caesura/>
             sindhūdbhavaṃ vāgnisamaṃ ca kṛtvā kṣiptvā ca mūtre sakṛdeva taptam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.34"> lauhaṃ ca kiṭṭaṃ bahuśaś ca taptvā nirvāpya mūtre
            bahuśas tathaiva |
            <caesura/>
             ekīkṛtaṃ gojalapiṣṭametadaikadhyamāvāpya pacedukhāyām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.35"> yathā na dahyeta tathā viśuṣkaṃ cūrṇīkṛtaṃ peyamudaśvitā
            tat |
            <caesura/>
             takraudanāśī vijayeta rogaṃ pāṇḍuṃ tathā dīpayate 'nalaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.36"> drākṣāguḍūcyāmalakīrasaiś ca siddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ
            lāgharake(lāghavake) hitaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             gauḍānariṣṭān madhuśarkarāś ca mūtrāsavān kṣārakṛtāṃs tathaiva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.37"> snigdhān rasānāmalakair upetān kolānvitān vāpi hi
            jāṅgalānām |
            <caesura/>
             seveta śophābhihitāṃś ca yogān pāṇḍvāmayī śāliyavāṃś ca nityam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.38"> śvāsātisārārucikāsamūrcchātṛṭchardiśūlajvaraśophadāhān |
            <caesura/>
             tathāvipākasvaramedasādān jayed yathāsvaṃ prasamīkṣya śāstram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.39"> anteṣu śūnaṃ parihīnamadhyaṃ mlānaṃ tathānteṣu ca
            madhyaśūnam |
            <caesura/>
             gude ca śephasyatha muṣkaśūnaṃ pratāmyamānaṃ ca visaṃjñakalpam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.40"> vivarjayet pāṇḍukinaṃ yaśo 'rthī tathātisārajvarapīḍitaṃ
            ca ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.44.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate
            kāyacikitsātantre pāṇḍurogapratiṣedho nāma (ṣaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) catuś
            catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||44 ||</l>
        </div>


        <div n="45" type="adhyāya">
          <head>pañcacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.1"> athāto raktapittapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.3"> krodhaśokabhayāyāsaviruddhān nātapānalān |
            <caesura/>
             kaṭvamlalabaṇakṣāratīkṣṇoṣṇātividāhinaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.4"> nityam abhyasato duṣṭo rasaḥ pittaṃ prakopayet |
            <caesura/>
             vidagdhaṃ svaguṇaiḥ pittaṃ vidahatyāśu śoṇitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.5"> tataḥ pravartate raktam ūrdhvaṃ cādho dvidhāpi vā |
            <caesura/>
             āmāśayād vrajed ūrdhvam adhaḥ pakvāśayād vrajet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.6ab"> vidagdhayor dvayoś cāpi dvidhā bhāgaṃ pravartate |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.6cd">kecit sayakṛtaḥ plīhnaḥ pravadanty asṛjo gatim || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.7ab"> ūrdhvaṃ sādhyam adho yāpyam asādhyaṃ yugapadgatam |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.7cd"> sadanaṃ śītakāmitvaṃ kaṇṭhadhūmāyanaṃ vamiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.8"> lohagandhiś ca niḥśvāso bhavaty asmin bhaviṣyati |
            <caesura/>
             bāhyāsṛglakṣaṇais tasya saṅkhyā doṣocchritīr viduḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.9"> daurbalyaśvāsakāsajvaravamathumadāstandritādāhamūrcchā
            bhukte cānne vidāhas tv adhṛtir api sadā hṛdyatulyā ca pīḍā |
            <caesura/>
             tṛṣṇā kaṇṭhasya bhedaḥ śirasi ca davanaṃ pūtiniṣṭhīvanaṃ ca dveṣo bhakte
            'vipāko viratir api rate raktapittopasargāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.10"> māṃsaprakṣālanābhaṃ kvathitam iva ca yat
            kardamāmbhonibhaṃ vā medaḥpūyāsrakalpaṃ yakṛd iva yadi vā pakvajambūphalābham
            |
            <caesura/>
             yat kṛṣṇaṃ yac ca nīlaṃ bhṛśam atikuṇapaṃ yatra coktā vikārās tad varjyaṃ
            raktapittaṃ surapatidhanuṣā yac ca tulyaṃ vibhāti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.11"> nādau saṃgrāhyam udriktaṃ yad asṛgbalino 'śnataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tat pāṇḍugrahaṇīkuṣṭhaplīhagulmajvarāvaham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.12"> adhaḥpravṛttaṃ vamanair ūrdhvagaṃ ca virecanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             jayed anyatarad vāpi kṣīṇasya śamanair asṛk || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.13"> atipravṛddhadoṣasya pūrvaṃ lohitapittinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             akṣīṇabalamāṃsāgneḥ kartavyamapatarpaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.14"> laṅghitasya tataḥ peyāṃ vidadhyāt svalpataṇḍulām |
            <caesura/>
             rasayūṣau pradātavyau surabhis nehasaṃskṛtau |
            <caesura/>
             tarpaṇaṃ pācanaṃ lehān sarpīṣi vividhāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.15"> drākṣāmadhukakāśmaryasitāyuktaṃ virecanam |
            <caesura/>
             yaṣṭīmadhukayuktaṃ ca sakṣaudraṃ vamanaṃ hitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.16"> payāṃsi śītāni rasāś ca jāṅgalāḥ satīnayūṣāś ca
            saśāliṣaṣṭikāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             paṭolaśelūsuniṣaṇṇayūthikāvaṭātimuktāṅkurasinduvārajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.17"> hitaṃ ca śākaṃ ghṛtasaṃskṛtaṃ sadā tathaiva
            dhātrīphaladāḍimānvitam |
            <caesura/>
             rasāś ca pārāvataśaṅkhakūrmajās tathā yavāgvo vihitā ghṛtottarāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.18"> santānikāś cotpalavargasādhite kṣīre praśastā
            madhuśarkarottarāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             himāḥ pradehā madhurā gaṇāś ca ye ghṛtāni pathyāni ca raktapittinām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.19"> madhūkaśobhāñjanakovidārajaiḥ priyaṅgukāyāḥ kusumaiś ca
            cūrṇitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhiṣag vidadhyāc caturaḥ samākṣikān hitāya lehānasṛjaḥ praśāntaye || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.20"> lihyāc ca dūrvāvaṭajāṃś ca pallavān madhudvitīyān
            sitakarṇikasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ ca kharjūraphalaṃ samākṣikaṃ phalāni cānyāny api tadguṇānyatha || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.21ab"> raktātisāraproktāṃś ca yogān atrāpi yojayet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.21cd">śuddhekṣukāṇḍam āpothya nave kumbhe himāmbhasā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.22"> yojayitvā kṣiped rātrāvākāśe sotpalaṃ tu tat |
            <caesura/>
             prātaḥ srutaṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ pibec choṇitapittavān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.23"> pibec chītakaṣāyaṃ vā jambvāmrārjunasaṃbhavam |
            <caesura/>
             udumbaraphalaṃ piṣṭvā pibet tad rasam eva vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.24"> trapuṣīmūlakalkaṃ vā sakṣaudraṃ taṇḍulāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             pibed akṣasamaṃ kalkaṃ yaṣṭīmadhukam eva vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.25"> candanaṃ madhukaṃ rodhram evam eva samaṃ pibet |
            <caesura/>
             karañjabījam evaṃ vā sitākṣaudrayutaṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.26"> majjānamiṅgudasyaivaṃ piben madhukasaṃyutam |
            <caesura/>
             sukhoṣṇaṃ lavaṇaṃ bījaṃ kārañjaṃ dadhimastunā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.27"> pibed vāpi tryahaṃ martyo raktapittābhipīḍitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             raktapittaharāḥ śastāḥ ṣaḍete yogasattamāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.28"> pathyāś caivāvapīḍeṣu ghrāṇataḥ prasrute 'sṛji |
            <caesura/>
             atinisrutarakto vā kṣaudrayuktaṃ pibed asṛk |
            <caesura/>
             yakṛd vā bhakṣayed ājamāmaṃ pittasamāyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.29"> palāśavṛkṣasvarase vipakvaṃ
            <caesura/>
             sarpiḥ pibet kṣaudrayutaṃ suśītam |
            <caesura/>
             vanaspatīnāṃ svarasaiḥ kṛtaṃ vā
            <caesura/>
             saśarkaraṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ pibed vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.30"> drākṣāmuśīrāṇy atha padmakaṃ sitā pṛthakpalāṃśānyudake
            samāvapet |
            <caesura/>
             sthitaṃ niśāṃ tadrudhir āmayaṃ jayet pītaṃ payo vāmbusamaṃ hitāśinaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.31"> turaṅgavarcaḥsvarasaṃ samākṣikaṃ pibet sitākṣaudrayutaṃ
            vṛṣasya vā |
            <caesura/>
             lihet tathā vāstukabījacūrṇaṃ kṣaudrānvitaṃ taṇḍulasāhvayaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.32"> lihyāc ca lājāñjanacūrṇamekamevaṃ sitākṣaudrayutāṃ
            tugākhyām |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāṃ sitāṃ tiktakarohiṇīṃ ca himāmbunā vā madhukena yuktām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.33ab"> pathyāmahiṃsrāṃ rajanīṃ ghṛtaṃ ca
            <caesura/>
             lihyāt tathā śoṇitapittarogī |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.33cd"> vāsākaṣāyotpalamṛtpriyaṅgurodhrāñjanāmbhoruhakeśarāṇi
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.34"> pītvā sitākṣaudrayutāni jahyāt pittasṛjo vegamudīrṇamāśu
            |
            <caesura/>
             gāyatrijambvarjunakovidāraśirīṣarodhrāśanaśālmalīnām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.35"> puṣpāṇi śigroś ca vicūrṇya leho madhvanvitaḥ
            śoṇitapittaroge |
            <caesura/>
             sakṣaudramindīvarabhasmavāri karañjabījaṃ madhusarpiṣī ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.36ab"> jambvarjunāmrakvathitaṃ ca toyaṃ ghnanti trayaḥ pittam
            asṛk ca yogāḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.36cd"> mūlāni puṣpāṇi ca mātuluṅgyāḥ piṣṭvā
            pibettaṇḍuladhāvanena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.37"> ghrāṇapravṛtte jalamāśu deyaṃ saśarkaraṃ nāsikayā payo
            vā |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣārasaṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ pibedvā saśarkaraṃ cekṣurasaṃ himaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.38"> śītopacāraṃ madhuraṃ ca kuryād
            <caesura/>
             viśeṣataḥ śoṇitapittaroge |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāghṛtakṣaudrasitāyutena
            <caesura/>
             vidārigandhādivipācitena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.39"> kṣīreṇa cāsthāpanam agryam uktaṃ
            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ ghṛtaṃ cāpy anuvāsanārtham |
            <caesura/>
             priyaṅgurodhrāñjanagairikotpalaiḥ
            <caesura/>
             suvarṇakālīyakaraktacandanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.40"> sitāśvagandhāmbudayaṣṭikāhvayair
            <caesura/>
             mṛṇālasaugandhikatulyapeṣitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nirūhya cainaṃ payasā samākṣikair
            <caesura/>
             ghṛtaplutaiḥ śītajalāvasecitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.41"> kṣīraudanaṃ bhuktam athānuvāsayed
            <caesura/>
             ghṛtena yaṣṭīmadhusādhitena ca |
            <caesura/>
             adhovahaṃ śoṇitameṣa nāśayet
            <caesura/>
             tathātisāraṃ rudhirasya dustaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.42"> virekayoge tvati caiva śasyate
            <caesura/>
             vāmyaś ca rakte vijite balānvitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.43"> evaṃvidhā uttarabāstayaś ca mūtrāśayasthe rudhire
            vidheyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pravṛttarakteṣu ca pāyujeṣu kuryād vidhānaṃ khalu raktapaittam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.44"> vidhiś cāsṛgdare 'pyeṣa strīṇāṃ kāryo vijānatā |
            <caesura/>
             śastrakarmaṇi raktaṃ ca yasyātīva pravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.45.45"> trayāṇām api doṣāṇāṃ śoṇite 'pi ca sarvaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             liṅgāny ālokya kartavyaṃ cikitsitam anantaram ||</l>
          <p xml:id="SS.6.45">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            raktapittapratiṣedho nāma (saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcacatvāriṃśattamo
            'dhyāyaḥ ||45 ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="46" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.1"> athāto mūrcchāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.3"> kṣīṇasya bahudoṣasya viruddhāhārasevinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vegāghātād abhīghātād dhīnasattvasya vā punaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.4"> karaṇāyataneṣūgrā bāhyeṣv ābhyantareṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             niviśante yadā doṣās tadā mūrcchanti mānavāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.5"> hṛtpīḍā jṛmbhaṇaṃ glāniḥ saṃjñānāśo balasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             sarvāsāṃ pūrvarūpāṇi yathāsvaṃ tā vibhāvayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.6"> saṃjñāvahāsu nāḍīṣu pihitāsvanilādibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tamo 'bhyupaiti sahasā sukhaduḥkhavyapohakṛt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.7"> sukhaduḥkhavyapohāc ca naraḥ patati kāṣṭhavat |
            <caesura/>
             moho mūrccheti tāṃ prāhuḥ ṣaḍvidhā sā prakīrtitā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.8"> vātādibhiḥ śoṇitena madyena ca viṣeṇa ca |
            <caesura/>
             ṣaṭsvapyetāsu pittaṃ hi prabhutvenāvatiṣṭhate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.9"> apasmāroktaliṅgāni tāsām uktāni tattvataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pṛthivyambhastamorūpaṃ raktagandhaś ca tanmayaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.10"> tasmād raktasya gandhena mūrcchanti bhuvi mānavāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dravyasvabhāva ity eke sthitās tu viṣamadyayoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.11"> guṇās tīvrataratvena sthitās tu viṣamadyayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ta eva tasmāj jāyeta mohas tābhyāṃ yatheritaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.11ef"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.12"> madyena vilapaṃś chete naṣṭavibhrāntamānasaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gātrāṇi vikṣipan bhūmau jarāṃ yāvan na yāti tat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.13"> vepathusvapnatṛṣṇāḥ syuḥ stambhaś ca viṣamūrcchite |
            <caesura/>
             veditavyaṃ tīvrataraṃ yathāsvaṃ viṣalakṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.14"> sekāvagāhau maṇayaḥ sahārāḥ śītāḥ pradehā vyajanānilāś
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             śītāni pānāni ca gandhavanti sarvāsu mūrcchāsvanivāritāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.15ab"> sitāpriyālekṣurasaplutāni drākṣāmadhūkasvarasānvitāni
            | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.15cd"> kharjūrakāśmaryarasaiḥ śṛtāni pānāni sarpīṃṣi ca
            jīvanāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.16"> siddhāni varge madhure payāṃsi sadāḍimā jāṅgalajā rasāś
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             tathā yavā lohitaśālayaś ca mūrcchāsu pathyāś ca sadā satīnāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.17"> bhujaṅgapuṣpaṃ maricānyuśīraṃ kolasya madhyaṃ ca pibet
            samāni |
            <caesura/>
             śītena toyena bisaṃ mṛṇālaṃ kṣaudreṇa kṛṣṇāṃ sitayā ca pathyām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.18"> kuryāc ca nāsāvadanāvarodhaṃ kṣīraṃ pibed vāpy atha
            mānuṣīṇām |
            <caesura/>
             mūrcchāṃ prasaktāṃ tu śirovirekairjayed abhīkṣṇaṃ vamanaiś ca tīkṣṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.19"> harītakīkvāthaśṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā dhātrīphalānāṃ svarasaiḥ
            kṛtaṃ vā |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāsitādāḍimalājavanti śītāni nīlotpalapadmavanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.20"> pibet kaṣāyāṇi ca gandhavanti pittajvaraṃ yāni śamaṃ
            nayanti |
            <caesura/>
             prabhūtadoṣas tamaso 'tirekāt saṃmūrcchito naiva vibudhyate yaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.21"> saṃnyastasaṃjño bhṛśaduś cikitsyo jñeyas tadā buddhimatā
            manuṣyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yathā maloṣṭaṃ salile niṣiktaṃ samuddhered āśvavilīnam eva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.21a"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.22ab"> tadvac cikitset tvarayā bhiṣak tam asvedanaṃ
            mṛtyuvaśaṃ prayātam | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.22cd"> tīkṣṇāñjanābhyañjanadhūmayogais tathā nakhābhyantarato
            trapātaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.23ab"> vāditragītānunayair apūrvair vighaṭṭanair
            guptaphalāvagharṣaiḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.23cd"> ābhiḥ kriyābhiś ca na labdhasaṃjñaḥ sānāhalālāśvasanaś
            ca varjyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.23ef"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.24ab"> prabuddhasaṃjñaṃ vamanānulomyaistīkṣṇair viśuddhaṃ
            laghupathyabhuktam | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.24cdef"> phalatrikaiś citrakanāgarāḍhyais tathāśmajātāj
            jatunaḥ prayogaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saśarkarair māsam upakrameta viśeṣato jīrṇaghṛtaṃ sa pāyyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.46.25"> yathāsvaṃ ca jvaraghnāni kaṣāyāṇyupayojayet |
            <caesura/>
             sarvamūrcchāparītānāṃ viṣajāyāṃ viṣāpaham ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            mūrcchāpratiṣedho nāma (aṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
            ||46 ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="47" type="adhyāya">
          <head>saptacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.1"> athātaḥ pānātyayapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.3"> madyamuṣṇaṃ tathā tīkṣṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ viśadam eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             rūkṣamāśukaraṃ caiva vyavāyi ca vikāśi ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.4"> auṣṇyācchītopacāraṃ tattaikṣṇyāddhanti manogatim |
            <caesura/>
             viśatyavayavān saukṣmyādvaiśadyātkaphaśukranut || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.5"> mārutaṃ kopayed raukṣyādāśutvāccāśukarmakṛt |
            <caesura/>
             harṣadaṃ ca vyavāyitvād vikāśitvād visarpati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.6"> tadamlaṃ rasataḥ proktaṃ laghu rocanadīpanam |
            <caesura/>
             kecillavaṇavarjyāṃs tu rasānatrādiśanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.7"> snigdhais tadannairmāṃsaiś ca bhakṣyaiś ca saha sevitam |
            <caesura/>
             bhavedāyuḥprakarṣāya balāyopacayāya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.8"> kāmyatā manasastuṣṭirdhairyaṃ tejo 'tivikramaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vidhivat sevyamāne tu madye sannihitā guṇāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.9"> tadevānannamajñena sevyamānamamātrayā |
            <caesura/>
             kayāgninā hy agnisamaṃ sametya kurute madam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.10"> madena karaṇānāṃ tu bhāvānyatve kṛte sati |
            <caesura/>
             nigūḍham api bhāvaṃ svaṃ prakāśīkurute 'vaśaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.11"> tryavasthaś ca mado jñeyaḥ pūrvo madhyo 'tha paś cimaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pūrve vīryaratiprītiharṣabhāṣyādivardhanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.12"> pralāpo madhyame moho yuktāyuktakriyās tathā |
            <caesura/>
             visaṃjñaḥ paś cime śete naṣṭakarmakriyāguṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.13"> ślaiṣmikānalpapittāṃś ca snigdhānmātropasevinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pānaṃ na bādhate 'tyarthaṃ viparītāṃs tu bādhate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.13-1"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.13-2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.13-3"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.13-4"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.13-5"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.14"> nirbhaktamekāntata eva madyaṃ niṣevyamāṇaṃ manujena
            nityam |
            <caesura/>
             utpādayet kaṣṭatamān vikārānāpādayec cāpi śarīrabhedam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.15"> kruddhena bhītena pipāsitena śokābhitaptena bubhukṣitena
            |
            <caesura/>
             vyāyāmabhārādhvaparikṣatena vegāvarodhābhihatena cāpi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.16"> atyamlabhakṣyāvatatodareṇa sājīrṇabhuktena tathābalena |
            <caesura/>
             uṣṇābhitaptena ca sevyamānaṃ karoti madyaṃ vividhān vikārān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.17"> pānātyayaṃ paramadaṃ pānājīrṇam athāpi vā |
            <caesura/>
             pānavibhramamugraṃ ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.18"> stambhāṅgamardhṛdayagrahatodakampāḥ pānātyaye 'nilakṛte
            śiraso rujaś ca |
            <caesura/>
             svedapralāpamukhaśoṣaṇadāhamūrcchāḥ pittātmake vadanalocanapītatā ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.19"> śleṣmātmake vamathuśītakaphaprasekāḥ sarvātmake bhavati
            sarvavikārasaṃpat |
            <caesura/>
             ūṣmāṇamaṅgagurutāṃ virasānanatvaṃ śleṣmādhikatvamaruciṃ malamūtrasaṅgam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.20"> liṅgaṃ parasya tu madasya vadanti tajjñāstṛṣṇāṃ rujāṃ
            śirasi sandhiṣu cāpi bhedam |
            <caesura/>
             ādhmānamudgiraṇamamlaraso vidāho 'jīrṇasya pānajanitasya vadanti liṅgam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.21"> jñeyāni tatra bhiṣajā suviniś citāni
            pittaprakopajanitāni ca kāraṇāni |
            <caesura/>
             hṛdgātratodavamathujvarakaṇṭhadhūmamūrcchākaphasravaṇamūrdharujo vidāhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.22"> dveṣaḥ surān navikṛteṣu ca teṣu teṣu taṃ pānavibhramam
            uśanty akhilena dhīrāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hīnottarauṣṭham atiśītam amandadāhaṃ tailaprabhāsyam atipānahataṃ
            (tailaprabhāsyam apipānahataṃ) vijahyāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.23"> jihvauṣṭhadantam asitaṃ tv athavāpi nīlaṃ pīte ca yasya
            nayane rudhiraprame ca |
            <caesura/>
             hikkājvarau vamathuvepathupārśvaśūlāḥ kāsabhramāvapi ca pānahataṃ bhajante || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.24"> teṣāṃ nivāraṇam idaṃhi mayocyamānaṃ
            vyaktābhidhānamakhilena vidhiṃ nibodha |
            <caesura/>
             madyaṃ tu cukramaricārdrakadīpyakuṣṭhasauvarcalāyutamalaṃ pavanasya śāntyai
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.25"> pṛthvīkadīpyakamahauṣadhahiṅgubhir vā sauvarcalena ca
            yutaṃ vitaret sukhāya |
            <caesura/>
             āmrātakāmraphaladāḍimamātuluṅgaiḥ kuryāc chubhāny api ca ṣaḍavapānakāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.26"> seveta vā phalarasopahitān rasādīnānūpavargapiśitāny api
            gandhavanti |
            <caesura/>
             pittātmake madhuravargakaṣāyamiśraṃ madyaṃ hitaṃ samadhuśarkaramiṣṭagandham
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.27"> pītvā ca madyam api cekṣurasapragāḍhaṃ niḥśeṣataḥ
            kṣaṇamavasthitamullikhec ca |
            <caesura/>
             lāvaiṇatittirirasāṃś ca pibedanamlān maudgān sukhāya saghṛtān sasitāṃś ca
            yūṣān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.28"> pānātyaye kaphakṛte kaphamullikhec ca madyena
            bimbividulodakasaṃyutena |
            <caesura/>
             seveta tiktakaṭukāṃś ca rasānudārān yūṣāṃś ca tiktakaṭukopahitān hitāya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.29"> pathyaṃ yavānnavikṛtāni ca jāṅgalāni śleṣmaghnamanyadapi
            yac ca niratyayaṃ syāt |
            <caesura/>
             kuryāc ca sarvamatha sarvabhave vidhānaṃ ddvandvodbhave dvayamavekṣya
            yathāpradhānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.30"> sāmānyamanyadapi yac ca samagramagryaṃ vakṣyāmi yac ca
            manaso madakṛt sukhaṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             tvaṅgāgapuṣpamagadhailamadhūkadhānyaiḥ ślakṣṇairajājimaricaiś ca kṛtaṃ
            samāṃśaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.31"> pānaṃ kapittharasavāriparūṣakāḍhyaṃ pānātyayeṣu
            vidhivatsrutamambarānte |
            <caesura/>
             hrīverapadmaparipelavasaṃprayuktaiḥ puṣpairvilipya karavīrajalodbhavaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.32"> piṣṭaiḥ sapadmakayutair api sārivādyaiḥ sekaṃ jalaiś ca
            vitaredamalaiḥ suśītaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tvakpatracocamaricailabhujaṅgapuṣpaśleṣmātakaprasavavalkaguḍair upetam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.33"> drākṣāyutaṃ hṛtamalaṃ madirāmayārtais tatpānakaṃ śuci
            sugandhi narairniṣevyam |
            <caesura/>
             piṣṭvā pibec ca madhukaṃ kaṭurohiṇīṃ ca drākṣāṃ ca mūlamasakṛt trapuṣībhavaṃ
            yat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.34"> kārpāsinīmatha ca nāgabalāṃ ca tulyāṃ pītvā sukhī
            bhavati sādhu suvarcalāṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             kāśmaryadāruviḍadāḍimapippalīṣu drākṣānvitāsu kṛtamambuni pānakaṃ yat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.35"> tadbījapūrakarasāyutamāśu pītaṃ śāntiṃ parāṃ paramade
            tvacirāt karoti |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāsitāmadhukajīrakadhānyakṛṣṇāsvevaṃ kṛtaṃ trivṛtayā ca pibettathaiva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.36"> sauvarcalāyutamudārarasaṃ phalāmlaṃ bhārgīśṛtena ca
            jalena hito 'vasekaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.37"> ikṣvākudhāmārgavavṛkṣakāṇi kākāhvayodumbarikāś ca dugdhe
            |
            <caesura/>
             vipācya tasyāñjalinā vameddhi madyaṃ pibec cāhni gate tvajīrṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.38"> tvakpippalībhujagapuṣpaviḍair upetaṃ seveta
            hiṅgumaricailayutaṃ phalāmlām |
            <caesura/>
             uṣṇāmbusaindhavayutāstvathavā viḍatvakcavyailahiṅgumagadhāphalamūlaśuṇṭhīḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.39"> hṛdyaiḥ khaḍair api ca bhojanamatra śastaṃ
            drākṣākapitthaphaladāḍimapānakaṃ yat |
            <caesura/>
             tat pānavibhramaharaṃ madhuśarkarāḍhyamāmrātakolarasapānakam eva cāpi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.40"> kharjūravetrakakarīraparūṣakeṣu drākṣātrivṛtsu ca kṛtaṃ
            sasitaṃ himaṃ vā |
            <caesura/>
             śrīparṇiyuktamathavā tu pibedimāni yaṣṭyāhvayotpalahimāmbuvimiśritāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.41">
            kṣīripravālabisajīrakanāgapuṣpapatrailavālusitasārivapadmakāni |
            <caesura/>
             āmrātabhavyakaramardakapitthakolavṛkṣāmlavetraphalajīrakadāḍimāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.42"> seveta vā
            maricajīrakanāgapuṣpatvakpatraviśvacavikailayutān rasāṃś ca |
            <caesura/>
             sūkṣmāmbarasrutahimāṃca sugandhigandhān pānodbhavānnudati saptagadānaśeṣān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.43"> pañcendriyārthaviṣayā mṛdupānayogā hṛdyāḥ sukhāś ca
            manasaḥ satataṃ niṣevyāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pānātyayeṣu vikaṭorunitambavatyaḥ pīnonnatastanabharānatamadhyadeśāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.44"> prauḍhāḥ striyo 'bhinavayauvanapīnagātryaḥ sevyāś ca
            pañcaviṣayātiśayasvabhāvāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.45"> pibedrasaṃ puṣpaphalodbhavaṃ vā
            sitāmadhūkatrisugandhiyuktam |
            <caesura/>
             saṃcūrṇya saṃyojya ca nāgapuṣpairajājikṛṣṇāmaricaiś ca tulyaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.46"> varṣābhūyaṣṭyāhvamadhūkalākṣātvakkarbudārāṅkurajīrakāṇi
            |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāṃ ca kṛṣṇāmatha keśaraṃ ca kṣīre samāloḍya pibet sukhepsuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.47"> bhavec ca madyena tu yena pātitaḥ prakāmapītena
            surāsavādinā |
            <caesura/>
             tad eva tasmai vidhivat pradāpayed viparyaye bhraṃśamavaśyamṛcchati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.48"> yathā narendropahatasya kasyacidbhavet prasādastata eva
            nānyataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dhruvaṃ tathā madyahatasya dehino bhavet prasādastata eva nānyataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.49"> vicchinnamadyaḥ sahasā yo 'timadyaṃ viṣevate |
            <caesura/>
             tasya pānātyayoddiṣṭā vikārāḥ saṃbhavanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.50"> madyasyāgneyavāyavyau guṇāvambuvahāni(guṇāvambhovahāni)
            tu |
            <caesura/>
             srotāṃsi śoṣayeyātāṃ tena tṛṣṇopajāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.51"> pāṭalotpalakandeṣu mudgaparṇyāṃ ca sādhitam |
            <caesura/>
             piben māgadhikonmiśraṃ tatrāmbho himaśītalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.52"> sarpistailavasāmajjadadhibhṛṅgarasairyutam |
            <caesura/>
             kvāthena bilvayavayoḥ sarvagandhaiś ca peṣitaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.53"> pakvam abhyañjane śreṣṭhaṃ seke kvāthaś ca śītalaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rasavanti ca bhojyāni yathāsvam avacārayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.54"> pānakāni suśītāni hṛdyāni surabhīṇi ca |
            <caesura/>
             tvacaṃ prāptas tu pānoṣmā pittaraktābhimūrcchitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dāhaṃ prakurute ghoraṃ pittavattatra bheṣajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.55"> śītaṃ vidhānamata ūrdhvamahaṃ pravakṣye
            dāhapraśāntikaramṛddhimatāṃ narāṇām |
            <caesura/>
             tatrādito malayajena hitaḥ pradehaś candrāṃśuhāratuhinodakaśītalena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.56"> śītāmbuśītalataraiś ca śayānamenaṃ
            hārairmṛṇālavalayairabalāḥ spṛśeyuḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhinnotpalojjvalahime śayane śayīta patreṣu vā sajalabinduṣu padminīnām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.57"> āsādayan pavanamāhṛtamaṅganābhiḥ
            kahlārapadmadalaśaivalasaṃcayeṣu |
            <caesura/>
             kāntairvanāntapavanaiḥ parimṛśyamānaḥ śaktaś caredbhavanakānanadīrghikāsu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.58"> dāhābhibhūtamathavā pariṣecayet tu
            lāmajjakāmburuhacandanatoyatoyaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             visrāvitāṃ hṛtamalāṃ navavāripūrṇāṃ padmotpalākulajalāmadhivāsitāmbum || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.59"> vāpīṃ bhajeta haricandanabhūṣitāṅgaḥ
            kāntākaraspṛśanakarkaśaromakūpaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tatrainamamburuhapatrasamaiḥ spṛśantyaḥ śītaiḥ karoruvadanaiḥ kaṭhinaiḥ
            stanaiś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.60"> toyāvagāhakuśalā madhurasvabhāvāḥ saṃharṣayeyurabalāḥ
            sukalaiḥ pralāpaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dhārāgṛhe pragalitodakadurdinābhe klāntaḥ śayīta salilānilaśītakukṣau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.61"> gandhodakaiḥ sakusumair upasiktabhūmau
            patrāmbucandanarasair upaliptakuḍye |
            <caesura/>
             jātyutpalapriyakakeśarapuṇḍarīkapunnāganāgakaravīrakṛtopacāre || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.62"> tasmin gṛhe kamalareṇvaruṇe śayīta
            yatnāhṛtānilavikampitapuṣpadāmni |
            <caesura/>
             hemantavindhyahimavanmalayācalānāṃ śītāmbhasāṃ sakadalīharitadrumāṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.63"> udbhinnanīlanalināmburuhākarāṇāṃ candrodayasya ca kathāḥ
            śṛṇuyānmanojñāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mlānaṃ pratāntamanasaṃ manaso 'nukūlāḥ pīnastanorujaghanā haricandanāṅgyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.64"> tā enamārdravasanāḥ saha saṃviśeyuḥ śliṣṭvāvalāḥ
            śithilamekhalahārayaṣṭyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.65"> harṣayeyurnaraṃ nāryaḥ svaguṇai rahasi sthitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tāḥ śaityāc chamayeyuś ca pittapānātyayāntaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.66"> tṛḍdāharaktapitteṣu kāryo 'yaṃ bheṣajakramaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sāmānyato viśeṣaṃ tu śṛṇu dāheṣv aśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.67"> kṛtsnadehānugaṃ raktamudriktaṃ dahati hy ati |
            <caesura/>
             saṃcūṣyate dahyate ca tāmrābhastāmralocanaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.68"> lohagandhāṅgavadano vahninevāvakīryate |
            <caesura/>
             taṃ vilaṅghya vidhānena saṃsṛṣṭāhāram ācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.69"> apraśāmyati dāhe ca rasais tṛptasya jāṅgalaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śākhāśrayā yathānyāyaṃ rohiṇīrvyadhayet sirāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.70"> pittajvarasamaḥ pittāt sa cāpy asya vidhir hitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tṛṣṇānirodhād abdhātau kṣīṇe tejaḥ samuddhatam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.71"> sabāhyābhyantaraṃ dehaṃ dahed vai mandacetasaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saṃśuṣkagalatālvoṣṭho jihvāṃ niṣkṛṣya ceṣṭate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.72"> tatropaśamayet tejas tv abdhātuṃ ca vivardhayet |
            <caesura/>
             pāyayet kāmam ambhaś ca śarkarāḍhyaṃ payo 'pi vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.73"> śītam ikṣurasaṃ manthaṃ vitarec ceritaṃ vidhim |
            <caesura/>
             asṛjā pūrṇakoṣṭhasya dāho bhavati duḥsahaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.74"> vidhiḥ sadyovraṇīyoktas tasya lakṣaṇam eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             dhātukṣayokto yo dāhas tena mūrcchātṛṣānvitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.75ab"> kṣāmasvaraḥ kriyāhīno bhṛśaṃ sīdati pīḍitaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.75cd"> raktapittavidhis tasya hitaḥ snigdho 'nilāpahaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.76"> kṣatajenāśnataś cānyaḥ śocato vāpy anekadhā |
            <caesura/>
             tenāntardahyate 'tyarthaṃ tṛṣṇāmūrcchāpralāpavān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.77"> tamiṣṭaviṣayopetaṃ suhṛdbhir abhisaṃvṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīramāṃsarasāhāraṃ vidhinoktena sādhayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.78"> marmābhighātajo 'py asti sa cāsādhyatamaḥ smṛtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarva eva ca varjyāḥ syuḥ śītagātreṣu dehiṣu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.79"> (evaṃvidho bhaved yas tu madirāmayapīḍitaḥ |)
            <caesura/>
             praśāntopadrave cāpi śodhanaṃ prāptam ācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.80"> sajīrakāṇyārdrakaśṛṅgaverasauvarcalāny ardhajalaplutāni
            |
            <caesura/>
             madyāni hṛdyānyatha gandhavanti pītāni sadyaḥ śamayanti tṛṣṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.47.81"> jalaplutaś candanabhūṣitāṅgaḥ sragvī sabhaktāṃ
            piśitopadaṃśām |
            <caesura/>
             piben surāṃ naiva labheta rogān manonuvighnaṃ ca madaṃ na yāti ||</l>


          <p xml:id="SS.6.47.trailer">iti suśrutasṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate
            kāyacikitsātantre madātyayapratiṣedho nāma (navamo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ)
            saptacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||47 ||</p>

        </div>


        <div n="48" type="adhyāya">
          <head>aṣṭacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.1"> athātas tṛṣṇāpratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.3"> satataṃ yaḥ pibedvāri na tṛptimadhigacchati |
            <caesura/>
             punaḥ kāṅkṣati toyaṃ ca taṃ tṛṣṇārditam ādiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.4"> sakṣobhaśokaśramamadyapānādrūkṣāmlaśuṣkoṣṇakaṭūpayogāt |
            <caesura/>
             dhātukṣayāllaṅghanasūryatāpāt pittaṃ ca vātaś ca bhṛśaṃ pravṛddhau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.5"> srotāṃsi saṃdūṣayataḥ sametau yānyambuvāhīni śarīriṇāṃ hi
            |
            <caesura/>
             srotaḥsvapāṃvāhiṣu dūṣiteṣu jāyeta tṛṣṇātibalā tatas tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.6"> tisraḥ smṛtāstāḥ kṣatajā caturthī kṣayāt tathānyām
            asamudbhavā ca |
            <caesura/>
             syāt saptamī bhaktanimittajā tu nibodha liṅgāny anupūrvaśas tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.7"> tālvoṣṭhakaṇṭhāsyaviśoṣadāhāḥ saṃtāpamohabhramavipralāpāḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             pūrvāṇi rūpāṇi bhavanti tāsām utpattikāleṣu viśeṣatas tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.8"> śuṣkāsyatā mārutasaṃbhavāyāṃ todas tathā śaṅkhaśiraḥsu
            cāpi |
            <caesura/>
             srotonirodho virasaṃ ca vaktraṃ śītabhir adbhiś ca vivṛddhim eti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.9"> mūrcchāpralāpārucivaktraśoṣāḥ pītekṣaṇatvaṃ pratataś ca
            dāhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śītābhikāṅkṣā mukhatiktatā ca pittātmikāyāṃ paridhūpanaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.10"> kaphāvṛtābhyāmanilānalābhyāṃ kapho 'pi śuṣkaḥ prakaroti
            tṛṣṇām |
            <caesura/>
             nidrā gurutvaṃ madhurāsyatā ca tayārditaḥ śuṣyati cātimātram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.11"> kaṇṭhopalepo mukhapicchilatvaṃ śītajvaraś
            chardirarocakaś ca |
            <caesura/>
             kaphātmikāyāṃ gurugātratā ca śākhāsu śophastvavipāka eva |
            <caesura/>
             etāni rūpāṇi bhavanti tasyāṃ tayārditaḥ kāṅkṣati nāti cāmbhaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.12"> kṣatasya rukśoṇitanirgamābhyāṃ tṛṣṇā caturthī kṣatajā
            matā tu |
            <caesura/>
             tayābhibhūtasya niśādināni gacchanti duḥkhaṃ pibato 'pi toyam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.13"> rasakṣayādyā kṣayajā matā sā tayārditaḥ śuṣyati dahyate
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             atyarthamākāṅkṣati cāpi toyaṃ tāṃ sannipātād itikecidāhuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.14"> rasakṣayoktāni ca lakṣaṇāni tasyāmaśeṣeṇa
            bhiṣagvyavasyet |
            <caesura/>
             tridoṣaliṅgāmasamudbhavā ca hṛcchūlaniṣṭhīvanasādayuktā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.15"> snigdhaṃ tathāmlaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca bhuktaṃ
            gurvannamevātitṛṣāṃ karoti |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīṇaṃ vicittaṃ badhiraṃ tṛṣārtaṃ vivarjayennirgatajihvamāśu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.16"> tṛṣṇābhivṛddhāvudare ca pūrṇe taṃ vāmayenmāgadhikodakena
            |
            <caesura/>
             vilobhanaṃ cātra hitaṃ vidheyaṃ syāddāḍimāmrātakamātuluṅgaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.17"> tisraḥ prayogairiha sannivāryāḥ śītaiś ca samyag
            rasavīryajātaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gaṇḍūṣamamlairvirase ca vaktre kuryāc chubhairāmalakasya cūrṇaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.18"> suvarṇarūpyādibhir agnitaptairloṣṭaiḥ kṛtaṃ vā
            sikatādibhir vā |
            <caesura/>
             jalaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ śamayet tu tṛṣṇāṃ saśarkaraṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ himaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.19"> pañcāṅgikāḥ pañcagaṇā ya uktāsteṣv ambu siddhaṃ prathame
            gaṇe vā |
            <caesura/>
             pibet sukhoṣṇaṃ manujo 'cireṇa tṛṣo vimucyeta hi vātajāyāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.20"> pittaghnavargais tu kṛtaḥ kaṣāyaḥ saśarkaraḥ
            kṣaudrayutaḥ suśītaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pītastṛṣāṃ pittakṛtāṃ nihanti kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ vāpy atha jīvanīyaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.21"> bilvāḍhakīkanyakapañcamūlīdarbheṣu siddhaṃ kaphajāṃ
            nihanti |
            <caesura/>
             hitaṃ bhavec chardanam eva cātra taptena nimbaprasavodakena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.22"> sarvāsu tṛṣṇāsvathavāpi paittaṃ kuryād vidhiṃ tena hi tā
            na santi |
            <caesura/>
             paryāgatodumbarajo rasas tu saśarkaratatkvathitodakaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.23"> vargasya siddhasya ca sārivādeḥ pātavyamambhaḥ śiśiraṃ
            tṛṣārtaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaśeruśṛṅgāṭakapadmamocabisekṣusiddhaṃ vāṃ nihanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.24"> lājotpalośīrakucandanāni dattvā pravāte niśi vāsayet tu
            |
            <caesura/>
             taduttamaṃ toyamudāragandhi sitāyutaṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ vadanti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.25"> drākṣāpragāḍhaṃ ca hitāya vaidyas tṛṣṇārditebhyo vitaren
            narebhyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sasārivādau tṛṇapañcamūle tathotpalādau prathame gaṇe ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.26"> kuryāt kaṣāyaṃ ca yatheritena madhūkapuṣpādiṣu cāpareṣu
            |
            <caesura/>
             rājādanakṣīrikapītaneṣu ṣaṭ pānakānyatra hitāni ca syuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.27"> satuṇḍikerāṇyathavā pibet tu piṣṭāni kārpāsasamudbhavāni
            |
            <caesura/>
             kṣatodbhavāṃ rugvinivāraṇena jayed rasānāmasṛjaś ca pānaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.28"> kṣayotthitāṃ kṣīraghṛtaṃ nihanyānmāṃsodakaṃ vā
            madhukodakaṃ vā |
            <caesura/>
             āmodbhavāṃ bilvavacāyutais tu jayet kaṣāyairatha dīpanīyaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.29"> āmrātabhallātabalāyutāni pibet kaṣāyāṇyatha dīpanāni |
            <caesura/>
             gurvannajātāṃ vamanairjayec ca kṣayādṛte sarvakṛtāṃ ca tṛṣṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.30"> śramodbhavāṃ māṃsaraso nihanti guḍodakaṃ vāpy athavāpi
            manthaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhaktoparodhāttṛṣito yavāgūmuṣṇāṃ piben manthamatho himaṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.31"> yā snehapītasya bhavec ca tṛṣṇā tatroṣṇamambhaḥ prapiben
            manuṣyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             madyodbhavāmardhajalaṃ nihanti madyaṃ tṛṣāṃ yāpi ca madyapasya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.32"> tṛṣṇodbhavāṃ hanti jalaṃ suśītaṃ saśarkaraṃ sekṣurasaṃ
            tathāmbhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             svaiḥ svaiḥ kaṣāyairvamanāni tāsāṃ tathā jvaroktāni ca pācanāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.48.33"> lepāvagāhau pariṣecanāni kuryāt tathā śītagṛhāṇi cāpi |
            <caesura/>
             saṃśodhanaṃ kṣīrarasau ghṛtāni sarvāsu lehānmadhurān himāṃś ca ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            (daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ āditaḥ) aṣṭacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||48 ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="49" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ekonapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.1"> athātaś chardipratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.3"> atidravairatisnigdhairahṛdyairlavaṇairati |
            <caesura/>
             akāle cātimātraiś ca tathāsātmyaiś ca bhojanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.4"> śramāt kṣayāt tathodvegād ajīrṇāt kṛmidoṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nāryāś cāpannasattvāyās tathātidrutam aśnataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.5"> atyantāmaparītasya chardervai saṃbhavo dhruvam |
            <caesura/>
             (bībhatsairhetubhiś cānyairdrutamutkleśito balāt ||) </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.6"> chādayannānanaṃ vegairardayannaṅgabhañjanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nirucyate chardir iti doṣo vaktrād viniścaran || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.7"> doṣānudīrayan vṛddhānudāno vyānasaṅgataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ūrdhvamāgacchati bhṛśaṃ viruddhāhārasevanāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.8"> praseko hṛdayotkleśo bhaktasyānabhinandanam |
            <caesura/>
             pūrvarūpaṃ mataṃ chardyā yathāsvaṃ ca vibhāvayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.9"> pracchardayet phenilamalpamalpaṃ śūlārdito
            'bhyarditapārśvapṛṣṭhaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śrāntaḥ saghoṣaṃ bahuśaḥ kaṣāyaṃ jīrṇe 'dhikaṃ sānilajā vamis tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.10"> yo 'mlaṃ bhṛśaṃ vā kaṭutiktavaktraḥ pītaṃ saraktaṃ
            haritaṃ vamedvā |
            <caesura/>
             sadāhacoṣajvaravaktraśoṣo mūrcchānvitaḥ pittanimittajā sā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.11"> yo hṛṣṭaromā madhuraṃ prabhūtaṃ śuklaṃ himaṃ
            sāndrakaphānuviddham |
            <caesura/>
             abhaktaruggauravasādayukto vamedvamī sā kaphakopajā syāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.12"> sarvāṇi rūpāṇi bhavanti yasyāṃ sā sarvadoṣaprabhavā matā
            tu |
            <caesura/>
             bībhatsajā dauhṛdajāmajā ca sātmyaprakopāt kṛmijā ca yā hi |
            <caesura/>
             sā pañcamī tāṃ ca vibhāvayet tu doṣocchrayeṇaiva yathoktamādau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.13"> śūlahṛllāsabahulā kṛmijā ca viśeṣataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kṛmihṛdrogatulyena lakṣaṇena ca lakṣitā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.14"> kṣīṇasyopadravairyuktāṃ sāsṛkpūyāṃ sacandrikām |
            <caesura/>
             chardiṃ prasaktāṃ kuśalo nārabheta cikitsitum || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.15"> āmāśayotkleśabhavā hi sarvāstasmād dhitaṃ laṅghanam eva
            tāsu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.16"> vamīṣu bahudoṣāsu chardanaṃ hitam ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             virecanaṃ vā kurvīta yathādoṣocchrayaṃ bhiṣak || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.17"> saṃsargaś cānupūrveṇa yathāsvaṃ bheṣajāyutaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             laghūni pariśuṣkāṇi sātmyānyannāni cācaret || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.18"> yathāsvaṃ ca kaṣāyāṇi jvaraghnāni prayojayet |
            <caesura/>
             hanyāt kṣīraghṛtaṃ pītaṃ chardiṃ pavanasaṃbhavām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.19"> sasaindhavaṃ pibet sarpirvātacchardinivāraṇam |
            <caesura/>
             mudgāmalakayūṣo vā sasarpiṣkaḥ sasaindhavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yavāgūṃ madhumiśrāṃ vā pañcamūlīkṛtāṃ pibet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.20"> pibedvā vyaktasindhūtthaṃ phalāmlaṃ vaiṣkiraṃ rasam |
            <caesura/>
             sukhoṣṇalavaṇaṃ cātra hitaṃ snehavirecanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.21"> pittopaśamanīyāni pākyāni śiśirāṇi ca |
            <caesura/>
             kaṣāyāṇyupayuktāni ghnanti pittakṛtāṃ vamīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.22"> śodhanaṃ madhuraiś cātra drākṣārasasam āyutaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             balavatyāṃ praśaṃsanti sarpis tailvakam eva ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.23"> āragvadhādiniryūhaṃ daśāṅgayogam eva vā |
            <caesura/>
             pāyayetātha sakṣaudraṃ kaphajāyāṃ cikitsakaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.24"> kṛtaṃ guḍūcyā vidhivat kaṣāyaṃ himasaṃjñitam |
            <caesura/>
             tisṛṣv api bhavet pathyaṃ mākṣikeṇa samanvitam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.25"> bībhatsajāṃ hṛdyatamairdauhṛdīṃ kāṅkṣitaiḥ phalaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             laṅghanairvamanaiś cāmāṃ sātmyaiḥ sātmyaprakopajām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.26"> kṛmihṛdrogavac cāpi kṛmijāṃ sādhayed vamīm |
            <caesura/>
             vitarec ca yathādoṣaṃ śastaṃ vidhimanantaram || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.27"> dadhittharasasṃsaktāṃ pippalīṃ mākṣikānvitām |
            <caesura/>
             muhurmuhurnaro līḍhvā chardibhyaḥ pravimucyate(pratimucyate) || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.28"> samākṣikā madhurasā pītā vā taṇḍulāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             tarpaṇaṃ vā madhuyutaṃ tisṛṇām api bheṣajam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.29"> svayaṅguptāṃ sayaṣṭyāhvāṃ taṇḍulāmbumadhudravām |
            <caesura/>
             pibed yavāgūm athavā siddhāṃ patraiḥ karañjajaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.30"> yuktāmlalavaṇāḥ piṣṭāḥ kustumburyo 'thavā hitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             taṇḍulāmbuyutaṃ khādet kapitthaṃ tryūṣaṇena vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.31"> sitācandanamadhvāktaṃ lihyād vā makṣikāśakṛt |
            <caesura/>
             pibet payo 'gnitaptaṃ ca nirvāpya gṛhagodhikām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.32"> sarpiḥkṣaudrayutān vāpi lājaśaktūn pibet tathā |
            <caesura/>
             sarpiḥkṣaudrasitopetāṃ māgadhīṃ vā lihet tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.33"> dhātrīrase candanaṃ vā ghṛṣṭaṃ mudgadalāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             kolāmalakamajjānaṃ lihyādvā trisugandhikam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.34"> sakṣaudrāṃ śālilājānāṃ yavagūṃ vā piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ghreyāṇyupaharec cāpi manoghrāṇasukhāni ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.49.35"> jāṅgalāni ca māṃsāni śubhāni pānakāni ca |
            <caesura/>
             bhojanāni vicitrāṇi kuryāt sarvāsvatandritaḥ ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            chardipratiṣedho nāma (ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ekonapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
            ||49 ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="50" type="adhyāya">
          <head>pañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.1"> athāto hikkāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.3"> vidāhiguruviṣṭambhir ūkṣābhiṣyandibhojanaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śītapānāsanasthānarajodhūmānilānalaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.4"> vyāyāmakarmabhārādhvavegāghātāpatarpaṇaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             āmadoṣābhighātastrīkṣayadoṣaprapīḍanaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.5"> viṣamāśanādhyanaśanais tathā samaśanair api |
            <caesura/>
             hikkā śvāsaś ca kāsaś ca nṛṇāṃ samupajāyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.6"> muhurmuhurvāyurudeti sasvano yakṛtplihāntrāṇi
            mukhādivākṣipan |
            <caesura/>
             sa ghoṣavānāśu hinastyasūn yatastatas tu hikketi bhiṣagbhir ucyate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.7"> annajāṃ yamalāṃ kṣudrāṃ gambhīrāṃ mahatīṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             vāyuḥ kaphenānugataḥ pañca hikkāḥ karoti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.8"> mukhaṃ kaṣāyamaratirgauravaṃ kaṇṭhavakṣasoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pūrvarūpāṇi hikkānāmāṭopo jaṭharasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.9"> tvaramāṇasya cāhāraṃ bhuñjānasyāthavā ghanam |
            <caesura/>
             vāyurannairavastīrṇaḥ kaṭukairardito bhṛśam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.10"> hikkayatyūrdhvago bhūtvā tāṃ vidyādannajāṃ bhiṣak |
            <caesura/>
             cireṇa yamalairvegairyā hikkā saṃpravartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.11"> kampayantī śirogrīvaṃ yamalāṃ tāṃ vinirdiśet |
            <caesura/>
             vikṛṣṭakālairyā vegairmandaiḥ samabhivartate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.12"> kṣudrikā nāma sā hikkā jatrumūlāt pradhāvitā |
            <caesura/>
             nābhipravṛttā yā hikkā ghorā gambhīranādinī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.13"> śuṣkauṣṭhakaṇṭhajihvāsyaśvāsapārśvarujākarī |
            <caesura/>
             anekopadravayutā gambhīrā nāma sā smṛtā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.14"> marmāṇyāpīḍayantīva satataṃ yā pravartate |
            <caesura/>
             dehamāyamya vegena ghoṣayatyatitṛṣyataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mahāhikketi sā jñeyā sarvagātraprakampinī || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.15"> āyamyate hikkato 'ṅgāni yasya dṛṣṭiś cordhvaṃ tāmyate
            yasya gāḍham |
            <caesura/>
             kṣīṇo 'nnadviṭ kāsate yaś ca hikkī tau dvāvantyau varjayed dhikkamānau || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.16"> prāṇāyāmodvejanatrāsanāni sūcītodaiḥ saṃbhramaś cātra
            śastaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yaṣṭyāhvaṃ vā mākṣikeṇāvapīḍe pippalyo vā śarkarācūrṇayuktāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.17"> sarpiḥ koṣṇaṃ kṣīramikṣo raso vā nātikṣīṇe chardanaṃ
            śāntihetoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nārīpayaḥpiṣṭamaśuklacandanaṃ ghṛtaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ ca sasaindhavaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.18"> cūrṇīkṛtaṃ saindhavamambhasāthavā nihanti hikkāṃ ca
            hitaṃ ca nasyataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yuñjyāddhūmaṃ śālaniryāsajātaṃ naipālaṃ vā goviṣāṇodbhavaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.19"> sarpiḥsnigdhaiś carmabālaiḥ kṛtaṃ vā hikkāsthāne
            svedanaṃ cāpi kāryam |
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudropetaṃ gairikaṃ kāñcanāhvaṃ lihyādbhasma grāmyasattvāsthijaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.20"> tadvacchvāvinmeṣagośalyakānāṃ(gośallakānāṃ)
            romāṇyantardhūmadagdhāni cātra |
            <caesura/>
             madhvājyāktaṃ barhipatraprasūtamevaṃ bhasmaudumbaraṃ tailvakaṃ vā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.21"> svarjikṣāraṃ bījapūrādrasena kṣaudropetaṃ hanti līḍhvāśu
            hikkām |
            <caesura/>
             sarpiḥsnigdhā ghnanti hikkāṃ yavāgvaḥ koṣṇagrāsāḥ pāyaso vā sukhoṣṇaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.22"> śuṇṭhītoye sādhitaṃ kṣīramājaṃ tadvat pītaṃ
            śarkarāsaṃyutaṃ vā |
            <caesura/>
             ātṛptervā sevyamānaṃ nihantyād ghrātaṃ hikkāmāśu mūtraṃ tvajāvyoḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.23"> sapūtikīṭaṃ laśunogragandhāhiṅgvabjamācūrṇya subhāvitaṃ
            tat |
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudraṃ sitāṃ vāraṇakeśaraṃ ca pibedrasenekṣumadhūkajena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.24"> pibet palaṃ vā lavaṇottamasya dvābhyāṃ palābhyāṃ haviṣaḥ
            samagram |
            <caesura/>
             harītakīṃ koṣṇajalānupānāṃ pibed ghṛtaṃ kṣāramadhūpapannam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.25"> rasaṃ kapitthānmadhupippalībhyāṃ śuktipramāṇaṃ prapibet
            sukhāya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.26"> kṛṣṇāṃ sitāṃ cāmalakaṃ ca līḍhaṃ saśṛṅgaveraṃ
            madhunāthavāpi |
            <caesura/>
             kolāsthimajjāñjanalājacūrṇaṃ hikkā nihanyānmadhunāvalīḍham || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.27"> pāṭalāyāḥ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ gairikaṃ kaṭurohiṇī |
            <caesura/>
             kharjūramadhyaṃ māgadhyaḥ kāśīśaṃ dadhināma ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.28"> catvāra ete yogāḥ syuḥ pratipādapradarśitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             madhudvitīyāḥ kartavyāste hikkāsu vijānatā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.29"> kapotapārāvatalāvaśaka(lla)śvadaṃṣṭragodhāvṛṣadaṃśajān
            rasān |
            <caesura/>
             pibet phalāmlānahimān sasaindhavān snigdhāṃs tathaiva rṣyamṛgadvijodbhavān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.50.30"> virecanaṃ pathyatamaṃ sasaindhavaṃ ghṛtaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ ca
            sitopalāyutam |
            <caesura/>
             sadāgatāvūrdhvagate 'nuvāsanaṃ vadanti kecic ca hitāya hikkinām ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            hikkāpratiṣedho nāma (dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) pañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||50
            ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="51" type="adhyāya">
          <head>ekapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.1"> athātaḥ śvāsapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.3"> yair eva kāraṇairhikkā bahubhiḥ saṃpravartate |
            <caesura/>
             tair eva kāraṇaiḥ śvāso ghoro bhavati dehinām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.4"> vihāya prakṛtiṃ vāyuḥ prāṇo 'tha kaphasaṃyutaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śvāsayatyūrdhvago bhūtvā taṃ śvāsaṃ paricakṣate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.5"> kṣudrakastamakaś chinno mahānūrdhvaś ca pañcadhā |
            <caesura/>
             bhidyate sa mahāvyādhiḥ śvāsa eko viśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.6"> prāgrūpaṃ tasya hṛtpīḍā bhaktadveṣo 'ratiḥ parā |
            <caesura/>
             ānāhaḥ pārśvayoḥ śūlaṃ vairasyaṃ vadanasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.7"> kiñcidārabhamāṇasya yasya śvāsaḥ pravartate |
            <caesura/>
             niṣaṇṇasyaiti śāntiṃ ca sa kṣudra iti saṃjñitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.8"> tṛṭsvedavamathuprāyaḥ kaṇṭhaghurghurikānvitaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viśeṣāddurdine tāmyec chvāsaḥ sa tamako mataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.9"> ghoṣeṇa mahatāviṣṭaḥ sakāsaḥ sakapho naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             yaḥ śvasity abalo 'nnadviṭ suptas tamakapīḍitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.10"> sa śāmyati kaphe hīne svapataś ca vidhardhate |
            <caesura/>
             mūrcchājvarābhibhūtasya jñeyaḥ pratamakas tu saḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.11"> ādhmāto dahyamānena bastinā sarujaṃ naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarvaprāṇena vicchinnaṃ śvasyācchinnaṃ tam ādiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.12"> niḥsaṃjñaḥ pārśvaśūlārtaḥ śuṣkakaṇṭho 'tighoṣavān |
            <caesura/>
             saṃrabdhanetrastvāyamya yaḥ śvasyāt sa mahān smṛtaḥ | </l>
          <l/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.13"> marmasv āyamyamāneṣu śvasan mūḍho muhuś ca yaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ūrdhvaprekṣī hataravas tam ūrdhvaśvāsam ādiśet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.14"> kṣudraḥ sādhyatamas teṣāṃ tamakaḥ kṛcchra ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             trayaḥ śvāsā na sidhyanti tamako durbalasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.15"> snehabastiṃ vinā kecidūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca śodhanam |
            <caesura/>
             mṛdu rāṇavatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śvāsināmādiśanti hi || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.16"> śvāse kāse ca hikkāyāṃ hṛdroge cāpi pūjitam |
            <caesura/>
             ghṛtaṃ purāṇaṃ saṃsiddhamabhayāviḍarāmaṭhaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.17"> sauvarcalābhayābilvaiḥ saṃskṛtaṃ vānavaṃ ghṛtam |
            <caesura/>
             pippalyādipratīvāpaṃ siddhaṃ vā prathame gaṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.18"> sapañcalavaṇaṃ sarpiḥ śvāsakāsau vyapohati |
            <caesura/>
             hiṃsrāviḍaṅgapūtīkatriphalāvyoṣacitrakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.19"> dvikṣīraṃ sādhitaṃ sarpiś caturguṇajalāplutam |
            <caesura/>
             kolamātraiḥ pibettaddhi śvāsakāsau vyapohati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.20"> arśāṃsyarocakaṃ gulmaṃ śakṛdbhedaṃ kṣayaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             kṛtsne vṛṣakaṣāye vā pacet sarpiś caturguṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.21"> tanmūlakusumāvāpaṃ śītaṃ kṣaudreṇa yojayet |
            <caesura/>
             śṛṅgīmadhūlikābhārgīśuṇṭhītārkṣyasitāmbudaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.22"> saharidraiḥ sayaṣṭyāhvaiḥ samairāvāpya yogataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ghṛtaprasthaṃ paceddhīmān śītatoye caturguṇe || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.23"> śvāsaṃ kāsaṃ tathā hikkāṃ sarpiretanniyacchati |
            <caesura/>
             suvahā kālikā bhargī śukākhyā naiculaṃ phalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.24"> kākādanī śṛṅgaveraṃ varṣabhūrbṛhatīdvayam |
            <caesura/>
             kolamātrairghṛtaprasthaṃ pacedebhir jaladvikam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.25"> kaṭūṣṇaṃ pītam etad dhi śvāsāmayavināśanam |
            <caesura/>
             sauvarcalayavakṣārakaṭukāvyoṣacitrakaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.26"> vacābhayāviḍaṅgaiś ca sādhitaṃ śvāsaśāntaye |
            <caesura/>
             gopavally udake siddhaṃ syād anyad dviguṇe ghṛtam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.27"> pañcaitāni havīṃṣyāhurbhiṣajaḥ śvāsakāsayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tālīśatāmalakyugrājīvantīkuṣṭhasaindhavaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.28"> bilvapuṣkarabhūtīkasauvarcalakaṇāgnibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             pathyā tejovatī yuktaiḥ sarpirjalacaturguṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.29"> hiṅgupādayutaṃ siddhaṃ sarvaśvāsaharaṃ param |
            <caesura/>
             vāsāghṛtaṃ ṣaṭpalaṃ vā ghṛtaṃ cātra hitaṃ bhavet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.30"> tailaṃ daśaguṇe siddhaṃ bhṛṅgarājarase śubhe |
            <caesura/>
             sevyamānaṃ yathānyāyaṃ śvāsakāsau vyapohati || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.31"> phalāmlā viṣkirarasāḥ snigdhāḥ pravyaktasaindhavāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             eṇādīnāṃ śirobhir vā kaulatthā vā susaṃskṛtāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.32"> hanyuḥ śvāsaṃ ca kāsaṃ ca saṃskṛtāni payāṃsi ca |
            <caesura/>
             timirasya ca bījāni karkaṭākhyā ca cūrṇitā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.33"> durālabhātha pippalyaḥ kaṭukākhyā harītakī |
            <caesura/>
             śvāvinmayūraromāṇi kolā māgadhikākaṇāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.34"> bhārgītvak śṛṅgaveraṃ ca śarkarā śallakāṅgajam |
            <caesura/>
             nṛttakauṇḍakabījāni cūrṇitāni tu kevalam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.35"> pañca ślokārdhikāstvete lehā ye samyag īritāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarpirmadhubhyāṃ te lehyāḥ kāsaśvāsārditairnaraiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.36"> saptacchadasya puṣpāṇi pippalīś cāpi mastunā |
            <caesura/>
             pibet saṃcūrṇya madhunā dhānāś cāpy atha bhakṣayet || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.37"> arkāṅkurairbhāvitānāṃ yavānāṃ sādhvanekaśaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tarpaṇaṃ vā pibedeṣāṃ sakṣaudraṃ śvāsapīḍitaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.38"> śirīṣakadalīkundapuṣpaṃ māgadhikāyutam |
            <caesura/>
             taṇḍulāmbuyutaṃ pītvā jayec chvāsānaśeṣataḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.39"> kolamajjāṃ tālamūlamṛṣyacarmamasīm api |
            <caesura/>
             lihyāt kṣaudreṇa bhārgīṃ vā sarpirmadhusamāyutām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.40"> nīcaiḥkadambabījaṃ vā sakṣaudraṃ taṇḍulāmbunā |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāṃ harītakīṃ kṛṣṇāṃ karkaṭākhyāṃ durālabhām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.41"> sarpirmadhubhyāṃ vilihan hanti śvāsān sudāruṇān |
            <caesura/>
             haridrāṃ maricaṃ drākṣāṃ guḍaṃ rāsnāṃ kaṇāṃ śaṭīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.42"> lihyāttailena tulyāni śvāsārto hitabhojanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             gavāṃ purīṣasvarasaṃ madhusarpiḥkaṇāyutam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.43"> lihyācchvāsseṣu kāseṣu vājināṃ vā śakṛdrasam |
            <caesura/>
             pāṇḍurogeṣu śotheṣu ye yogāḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.44"> śvāsakāsāpahāste 'pi kāsaghnā ye ca kīrtitāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhārgītvak tryūṣaṇaṃ tailaṃ haridrāṃ kaṭurohiṇīm || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.45"> pippalīṃ maricaṃ caṇḍāṃ gośakṛdrasam eva ca |
            <caesura/>
             talakoṭasya bījeṣu pacedutkārikāṃ śubhām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.46"> sevyamānā nihantyeṣā śvāsānāśu sudustarān |
            <caesura/>
             purāṇasarpiḥ pippalyaḥ kaulatthā jāṅgalā rasāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.47"> surā sauvīrakaṃ hiṅgu mātuluṅgaraso madhu |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāmalakabilvāni śastāni śvāsihikkinām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.48"> śvāsahikkāparigataṃ snigdhaiḥ svedair upācaret |
            <caesura/>
             āktaṃ lavaṇatailābhyāṃ tairasya grathitaḥ kaphaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.49"> khastho vilayanaṃ yāti mārutaś ca praśāmyati |
            <caesura/>
             svinnaṃ jñātvā tataś caiva bhojayitvā rasaudanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.50"> vātaśleṣmavibandhe vā bhiṣag dhūmaṃ prayojayet |
            <caesura/>
             manaḥśilādevadāruharidrācchadanāmiṣaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.51"> lākṣorubūkamūlaiś ca kṛtvā vartīr vidhānataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarpiryavamadhūcchiṣṭaśālaniryāsajaṃ tathā || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.52"> śṛṅgabālakhurasnāyutvak samastaṃ gavām api |
            <caesura/>
             turuṣkaśallakīnāṃ ca gugguloḥ padmakasya ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.53"> ete sarve sasarpiṣkā dhūmāḥ kāryā vijānatā |
            <caesura/>
             balīyasi kaphagraste vamanaṃ savirecanam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.54"> durbale caiva rūkṣe ca tarpaṇaṃ hitam ucyate |
            <caesura/>
             jāṅgalorabhrajairmāṃsairānūpair vā susaṃskṛtaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.55"> nidigdhikāṃ cāmalakapramāṇāṃ hiṅgvardhayuktāṃ madhunā
            suyuktām |
            <caesura/>
             lihan naraḥ śvāsanipīḍito hi śvāsaṃ jayaty eva balāttryaheṇa || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.51.56"> yathāgniriddhaḥ pavanānuviddho vajraṃ yathā vā
            surarājamuktam |
            <caesura/>
             rogāstathaite khalu durnivārāḥ śvāsaś ca kāsaś ca vilambikā ca ||</l>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            hikkāśvāsapratiṣedho nāma (tryodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) ekapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
            ||51 ||</p>
        </div>

        <div n="52" type="adhyāya">
          <head>dvipañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.1"> athātaḥ kāsapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.3"> uktā ye hetavo nṝṇāṃ rogayoḥ śvāsahikkayoḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kāsasyāpi ca vijñeyāsta evotpattihetavaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.4"> dhūmopaghātādrajasas tathaiva vyāyāmarūkṣānnaniṣevaṇāc ca
            |
            <caesura/>
             vimārgagatvād api bhojanasya vegāvarodhāt kṣavathos tathaiva || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.5"> prāṇo hyudānānugataḥ praduṣṭaḥ
            saṃbhinnakāṃsyasvanatulyaghoṣaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nireti vaktrāt sahasā sadoṣaḥ kāsaḥ sa vidvadbhir udāhṛtas tu || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.6"> sa vātapittaprabhavaḥ kaphāc ca kṣatāttathānyaḥ kṣayajo
            'paraś ca |
            <caesura/>
             pañcaprakāraḥ kathito bhiṣagbhir vivardhito yakṣmavikārakṛt syāt || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.7"> bhaviṣyatas tasya tu kaṇṭhakaṇḍūrbhojyoparodho
            galatālulepaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             svaśabdavaiṣamyamarocako 'gnisādaś ca liṅgāni bhavantyamūni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.8"> hṛcchaṅkhamūrdhodarapārśvaśūlī kṣāmānanaḥ
            kṣīṇabalasvaraujāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prasaktamantaḥkaphamīraṇena kāset tu śuṣkaṃ svarabhedayuktaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.9"> urovidāhajvaravaktraśoṣairabhyarditastiktamukhastṛṣārtaḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             pittena pītāni vamet kaṭūni kāset sa pāṇḍuḥ paridahyamānaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.10"> pralipyamānena(vilipyamānena) mukhena sīdan śirorujārtaḥ
            kaphapūrṇadehaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             abhaktaruggauravasādayuktaḥ kāseta nā sāndrakaphaṃ kaphena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.11"> vakṣo 'timātraṃ vihataṃ tu yasya
            vyāyāmabhārādhyayanābhighātaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             viśliṣṭavakṣāḥ sa naraḥ saraktaṃ ṣṭhīvatyabhīkṣṇaṃ kṣatajaṃ tamūhuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.12"> sa gātraśūlajvaradāhamohān prāṇakṣayaṃ copalabheta kāsī
            |
            <caesura/>
             śuṣyan viniṣṭhīvati durbalas tu prakṣīṇamāṃso rudhiraṃ sapūyam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.13"> sasarvaliṅgaṃ bhṛśaduś cikitsyaṃ cikitsitajñāḥ kṣayajaṃ
            vadanti |
            <caesura/>
             vṛddhatvamāsādya bhavet tu yo vai yāpyaṃ tamāhurbhiṣajas tu kāsam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.14">
            śṛṅgīvacākaṭphalakattṛṇābdadhānyābhayābhārgyamarāhvaviśvam |
            <caesura/>
             uṣṇāmbunā hiṅguyutaṃ tu pītvā baddhāsyamapyāśu jahāti kāsam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.15"> phalatrikavyoṣaviḍaṅgaśṛṅgīrāsnāvacāpadmakadevakāṣṭhaiḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             lehaḥ samaiḥ kṣaudrasitāghṛtāktaḥ kāsaṃ nihanyādacirādudīrṇam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.16"> pathyāṃ sitāmāmalakāni lājāṃ samāgadhīṃ cāpi vicūrṇya
            śuṇṭhīm |
            <caesura/>
             sarpirmadhubhyāṃ vilihīta kāsī sasaindhavāṃ voṣṇajalena kṛṣṇām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.17"> khādedguḍaṃ nāgarapippalībhyāṃ drākṣāṃ ca
            sarpirmadhunāvalihyāt |
            <caesura/>
             drākṣāṃ sitāṃ māgadhikāṃ ca tulyāṃ saśṛṅgaveraṃ madhukaṃ tugāṃ ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.18"> lihyād ghṛtakṣaudrayutāṃ samāṃśāṃ sitopalāṃ vā
            maricāṃśayuktām |
            <caesura/>
             dhātrīkaṇāviśvasitopalāś ca saṃcūrṇya maṇḍena pibec ca dadhnaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.19"> hareṇukāṃ māgadhikāṃ ca tulyāṃ dadhnā pibet
            kāsagadābhibhūtaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ubhe haridre suradāruśuṇṭhīṃ gāyatrisāraṃ ca pibet samāṃśam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.20"> bastasya mūtreṇa sukhāmbunā vā dantīṃ dravantīṃ ca
            satilvakākhyām |
            <caesura/>
             bhṛṣṭāni sarpīṃṣyatha bādarāṇi khādet palāśāni sasaindhavāni || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.21"> kolapramāṇaṃ prapibeddhi hiṅgu sauvīrakeṇāmlarasena vāpi
            |
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudreṇa lihyānmaricāni vāpi bhārgīvacāhiṅgukṛtā ca vartiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.22"> dhūme praśastā ghṛtasaṃprayuktā veṇutvagelālavaṇaiḥ kṛtā
            vā |
            <caesura/>
             musteṅgudītvaṅmadhukāhvamāṃsīmanaḥśilālaiś chagalāmbupiṣṭaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.23"> vidhāya vartīś ca payo 'nupānaṃ dhūmaṃ
            pibedvātabalāsakāsī |
            <caesura/>
             pibec ca sīdhuṃ maricānvitaṃ vā tenāśu kāsaṃ jayati prasahya || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.24"> drākṣāmbumañjiṣṭhapurāhvayābhiḥ kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ
            mākṣikasaṃprayuktam |
            <caesura/>
             nidigdhikānāgarapippalībhiḥ khādec ca mudgānmadhunā susiddhān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.25"> utkārikāṃ sarpiṣi nāgarāḍhyāṃ paktvā
            samūlaistruṭikolapatraiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ebhir niṣeveta kṛtāṃ ca peyāṃ tanvīṃ suśītāṃ madhunā vimiśrām || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.26"> yat plīhni sarpirvihitaṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ tadvātakāsaṃ jayati
            prasahya |
            <caesura/>
             vidārigandhādikṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ vā rasena vā vāsakajena pakvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.27"> virecanaṃ snaihikamatra coktamāsthāpanaṃ cāpy anuvāsanaṃ
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             dhūmaṃ pibet snaihikamapramattaḥ pibet sukhoṣṇaṃ ghṛtam eva cātra || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.28"> hitā yavāgvaś ca raseṣu siddhāḥ payāṃsi lehāḥ saghṛtās
            tathaiva |
            <caesura/>
             pracchardanaṃ kāyaśirovirekās tathaiva dhūmāḥ kavalagrahāś ca || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.29"> uṣṇāś ca lehāḥ kaṭukā nihanyuḥ kaphaṃ viśeṣeṇa viśoṣaṇaṃ
            ca |
            <caesura/>
             kaṭutrikaṃ cāpi vadanti pathyaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṛmighnasvarase vipakvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.30"> nirguṇḍipatrasvarase ca pakvaṃ sarpiḥ kaphotthaṃ
            vinihanti kāsam |
            <caesura/>
             pāṭhāviḍavyoṣaviḍaṅgasindhutrikaṇṭarāsnāhutabhugbalābhiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.31"> śṛṅgīvacāmbhodharadevadārudurālabhābhārgyabhayaśaṭībhiḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             samyag vipakvaṃ dviguṇena sarpirnidigdhikāyāḥ svarasena caitat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.32"> śvāsāgnisādasvarabhedabhinnānnihantyudīrṇānapi pañca
            kāsān |
            <caesura/>
             vidārigandhotpalasārivādīn niṣkvāthya vargaṃ madhuraṃ ca kṛtsnam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.33"> ghṛtaṃ pacedikṣurasāmbudugdhaiḥ kākolivarge ca
            saśarkaraṃ tat |
            <caesura/>
             prātaḥ pibet pittakṛte ca kāse ratiprasūte kṣataje ca kāse || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.34"> kharjūrabhārgīmagadhāpriyālamadhūlikailāmalakaiḥ
            samāṃśaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇaṃ sitākṣaudraghṛtaprāgāḍhaṃ trīn hanti kāsānupayujyamānam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.35"> raktāharidrāñjanavahnipāṭhāmūrvopakulyā vilihet samāṃśāḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             kṣaudreṇa kāse kṣataje kṣayotthe pibed ghṛtaṃ cekṣurase vipakvam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.36"> cūrṇaṃ pibed āmalakasya vāpi kṣīreṇa pakvaṃ saghṛtaṃ
            hitāśī |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇāni godhūmayavodbhavāni kākolivargaś ca kṛtaḥ susūkṣmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.37"> kāseṣu peyastriṣu kāsavadbhiḥ kṣīreṇa sakṣaudraghṛtena
            vāpi |
            <caesura/>
             guḍodakaṃ vā kvathitaṃ pibeddhi kṣaudreṇa śītaṃ maricopadaṃśam || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.38"> prasthatrayeṇāmalakīrasasya śuddhasya dattvārdhatulāṃ
            guḍasya |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇīkṛtairgranthikacavyajīravyoṣebhakṛṣṇāhapuṣājamodaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.39"> viḍaṅgasindhutriphalāyavānīpāṭhāgnidhānyaiś ca
            picupramāṇaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             dattvā trivṛccūrṇapalāni cāṣṭāvaṣṭau ca tailasya pacedyathāvat || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.40"> taṃ bhakṣayed akṣaphalapramāṇaṃ
            yatheṣṭaceṣṭastrisugandhiyuktam |
            <caesura/>
             anena sarve grahaṇīvikārāḥ saśvāsakāsasvarabhedaśothāḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.41"> śāmyanti cāyaṃ ciramantaragnerhatasya puṃstvasya ca
            vṛddhihetuḥ |
            <caesura/>
             strīṇāṃ ca vandhyāmayanāśanaḥ syāt kalyāṇako nāma guḍaḥ pratītaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.42"> dvipañcamūlebhakaṇātmaguptābhārgīśaṭīpuṣkaramūlaviśvān |
            <caesura/>
             pāṭhāmṛtāgranthikaśaṅkhapuṣpīrāsnāgnyapāmārgabalāyavāsān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.43"> dvipālikān nyasya yavāḍhakaṃ ca harītakīnāṃ ca śataṃ
            gurūṇām |
            <caesura/>
             droṇe jalasyāḍhakasaṃyute ca kvāthe kṛte pūtacaturthabhāge || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.44"> pacettulāṃ śuddhaguḍasya dattvā pṛthak ca tailāt kuḍavaṃ
            ghṛtāc ca |
            <caesura/>
             cūrṇaṃ ca tāvan magadhodbhavāyā deyaṃ ca tasmin madhu siddhaśīte || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.45"> rasāyanāt karṣamato vilihyāddve cābhaye nityam athāśu
            hanyāt |
            <caesura/>
             tad rājayakṣmagrahaṇīpradoṣaśophāgnimāndyasvarabhedakāsān || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.46"> pāṇḍvāmayaśvāsaśirovikārān hṛdrogahikkāviṣam ajvarāṃś ca
            |
            <caesura/>
             medhābalotsāham atipradaṃ ca cakāra caitad bhagavān agastyaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.52.47"> kulīraśuktīcaṭakaiṇalāvānniṣkvāthya vargaṃ madhuraṃ ca
            kṛtsnam |
            <caesura/>
             pacedghṛtaṃ tat tu niṣevyamāṇaṃ hanyāt kṣatotthaṃ kṣayajaṃ ca kāsam ||
            śatāvarīnāgabalāvipakvaṃ ghṛtaṃ vidheyaṃ ca hitāya kāsinām | </l>
          <l/>
          <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyām uttaratantrāntargate kāyacikitsātantre
            kāsapratiṣedho nāma (caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ, āditaḥ) dvipañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||52
            ||</p>
        </div>


        <div n="53" type="adhyāya">

          <head>tripañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ | </head>
          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.1"> athātaḥ svarabhedapratiṣedham adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.3"> atyuc cabhāṣaṇaviṣādhyayanātigītaśītādibhiḥ prakupitāḥ
            pavanādayas tu |
            <caesura/>
             srotaḥsu te svaravaheṣu gatāḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ hanyuḥ svaraṃ bhavati cāpi hi
            ṣaḍvidhaḥ saḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.4"> vātena kṛṣṇanayanānanamūtravarcā bhinnaṃ śanair vadati
            gadgadavat svaraṃ ca |
            <caesura/>
             pittena pītavadanākṣipurīṣamūtro brūyād galena paridāhasamanvitena || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.5"> kṛcchrāt kaphena satataṃ kapharuddhakaṇṭho mandaṃ
            śanairvadati cāpi divā viśeṣaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sarvātmake bhavati sarvavikārasaṃpadavyaktatā ca vacasastamasādhyam āhuḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.6"> dhūpyeta vāk kṣayakṛte kṣayamāpnuyāc ca vāgeṣa cāpi(vāpi)
            hatavāk parivarjanīyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             antargalaṃ svaramalakṣyapadaṃ cireṇa medaś cayādvadati digdhagalauṣṭhatāluḥ
            || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.53.7"> kṣīṇasya vṛddhasya kṛśasya cāpi cirotthito yaś ca
            sahopajātaḥ |
            <caesura/>
